## 41. MSH6通过调控cGAS的胞质/核分布来调节其在抗病毒和抗肿瘤信号通路中的活性。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41824461)
**期刊：** Cell reports
**PMID：** 41824461
**DOI：** 10.1016/j.celrep.2026.117059

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** MSH6 regulates cGAS activity in antiviral and antitumor signaling pathways by governing its cytosolic/nuclear distribution.

> **英文摘要：**
> While the cytosolic localization of cGAS is critical for cells to initiate immune responses and protect cells from viral infections, the activity of cGAS in the nucleus is inhibited to prevent autoimmune responses triggered by self-DNA. Therefore, the dynamically regulated distribution of cGAS in the cytosol and nucleus ensures its precise role in maintaining immune homeostasis. However, the molecular mechanism governing this spatial distribution of cGAS remains unclear. Here, we identify MSH6 as a regulator promoting cGAS nuclear localization by enhancing its association with importin-α proteins, consequently reducing cGAS condensation and activity. We further show that MSH6 attenuates antitumor immunity and that its deficiency in tumor cells leads to an effective tumor eradication by heat-inactivated modified vaccinia virus Ankara. Collectively, our results not only provide insights into understanding how cGAS activity is regulated but also suggest a therapeutic potential for treating MSH6-mutated tumors through the cGAS-mediated signaling pathway.

> **中文摘要：**
> cGAS在胞质中的定位对于细胞启动免疫反应、抵御病毒感染至关重要，而其核内活性则受到抑制，以防止自身DNA引发的自身免疫反应。因此，cGAS在胞质和细胞核中动态调节的分布确保了其在维持免疫稳态中的精确作用。然而，调控cGAS这种空间分布的分子机制尚不清楚。本研究鉴定出MSH6是一个通过增强cGAS与importin-α蛋白的结合来促进cGAS核定位的调节因子，从而减少cGAS的凝聚及其活性。我们进一步证明，MSH6会削弱抗肿瘤免疫，而肿瘤细胞中MSH6的缺失会导致热灭活改良安卡拉痘苗病毒有效清除肿瘤。总之，我们的研究结果不仅为理解cGAS活性如何被调控提供了见解，也提示了通过cGAS介导的信号通路治疗MSH6突变肿瘤的潜在治疗可能性。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在阐明调控cGAS胞质/核分布的关键分子机制及其在抗病毒与抗肿瘤免疫中的功能。研究者通过分子生物学方法，鉴定出DNA错配修复蛋白MSH6是促进cGAS核定位的关键调节因子，其机制是增强cGAS与核输入蛋白importin-α的结合。核心发现是MSH6通过将cGAS限制在核内、抑制其凝聚与活性，从而负向调控抗肿瘤免疫；其缺失则使肿瘤对热灭活病毒疗法敏感。该研究的创新性在于首次将MSH6与cGAS的空间调控及天然免疫信号联系起来，为治疗MSH6突变型肿瘤提供了新的潜在靶点；局限性在于主要发现基于体外和动物模型，其临床转化潜力及在更广泛肿瘤类型中的普适性有待进一步验证。

## 42. 靶向DSTYK-ULK1轴重塑TNFR1信号通路以克服肺癌治疗耐药

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41824459)
**期刊：** Cell reports
**PMID：** 41824459
**DOI：** 10.1016/j.celrep.2026.117087

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Targeting the DSTYK-ULK1 axis rewires TNFR1 signaling to overcome treatment resistance in lung cancer.

> **英文摘要：**
> Immunotherapy has transformed the treatment of non-small cell lung cancer (NSCLC). Yet, acquired resistance remains a major clinical challenge. Defining molecular determinants of tumor sensitivity to T cell-mediated killing is therefore critical. Tumor necrosis factor α (TNF-α) released by cytotoxic T cells promotes tumor细胞死亡, whereas NF-κB signaling supports survival. Autophagy counteracts TNFα-induced apoptosis, and its inhibition enhances responses to immune checkpoint inhibitors (ICIs). Genomic alterations further contribute to immune evasion and reduced immunotherapy efficacy. We previously identified DSTYK, a dual serine/threonine and tyrosine kinase amplified in NSCLC, as a suppressor of TNF-α-mediated CD8 T cell killing and a driver of ICI resistance through autophagy. Here, we show that DSTYK modulates TNFR1 signaling by phosphorylating the autophagy initiator ULK1, which enables ULK1-dependent phosphorylation of RIPK1. Loss of DSTYK disrupts ULK1 activation, promotes RIPK1 autophosphorylation, proapoptotic signaling, and impaired NF-κB-dependent survival. These findings define a DSTYK-ULK1-RIPK1 axis controlling TNF-α-induced apoptosis and support targeting ULK1 to sensitize DSTYK-amplified NSCLC to T cell-mediated killing.

> **中文摘要：**
> 免疫疗法已经改变了非小细胞肺癌（NSCLC）的治疗格局。然而，获得性耐药仍然是一个主要的临床挑战。因此，明确肿瘤对T细胞介导杀伤敏感性的分子决定因素至关重要。细胞毒性T细胞释放的肿瘤坏死因子α（TNF-α）促进肿瘤细胞死亡，而NF-κB信号通路则支持细胞存活。自噬拮抗TNFα诱导的细胞凋亡，抑制自噬可增强对免疫检查点抑制剂（ICIs）的反应。基因组改变进一步促进了免疫逃逸并降低了免疫疗法的疗效。我们先前发现，在NSCLC中扩增的双重丝氨酸/苏氨酸和酪氨酸激酶DSTYK，是TNF-α介导的CD8 T细胞杀伤的抑制因子，并通过自噬驱动ICI耐药。本研究显示，DSTYK通过磷酸化自噬启动因子ULK1来调节TNFR1信号传导，这使ULK1能够依赖性地磷酸化RIPK1。DSTYK的缺失破坏了ULK1的激活，促进了RIPK1的自磷酸化、促凋亡信号传导，并损害了NF-κB依赖的存活。这些发现定义了一个控制TNF-α诱导细胞凋亡的DSTYK-ULK1-RIPK1轴，并支持靶向ULK1以使DSTYK扩增的NSCLC对T细胞介导的杀伤敏感。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在解析NSCLC免疫治疗耐药的分子机制，并探索克服策略。通过分子生物学方法，揭示了DSTYK激酶通过磷酸化ULK1并进而调控RIPK1磷酸化状态，从而在TNF-α信号通路中平衡细胞凋亡与生存的关键作用。其核心创新性在于发现并验证了DSTYK-ULK1-RIPK1这一全新的信号轴，为DSTYK扩增型NSCLC患者提供了通过靶向ULK1来逆转免疫治疗耐药的理论基础和潜在治疗靶点。局限性在于研究主要基于机制探索，其临床转化效果和安全性尚需后续体内及临床研究进一步验证。

## 43. IRE1α通过降解NR1D1 mRNA和调控溶酶体生物发生来调节免疫性血小板减少症中的巨噬细胞吞噬作用。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41824452)
**期刊：** Cell reports
**PMID：** 41824452
**DOI：** 10.1016/j.celrep.2026.117083

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** IRE1α regulates macrophage phagocytosis in immune thrombocytopenia through NR1D1 mRNA decay and lysosomal biogenesis.

> **英文摘要：**
> Macrophage phagocytosis is essential for immune homeostasis but must be tightly constrained to prevent pathological tissue damage. How cellular stress pathways enforce phagocytic homeostasis remains incompletely understood. Here, we show that phagocytosis selectively activates the endoplasmic reticulum stress sensor IRE1α in macrophages, which functions as a negative regulator of lysosome-driven phagocytic amplification. Using myeloid-specific IRE1α-deficient mice and pharmacological inhibition, we demonstrate that loss of IRE1α RNase activity leads to excessive phagocytosis through unchecked lysosomal biogenesis. Mechanistically, phagocytosis-activated IRE1α directly degrades Nr1d1 mRNA via regulated IRE1α-dependent decay (RIDD), thereby restraining NR1D1-driven lysosomal expansion. Disruption of this IRE1α-NR1D1 axis exacerbates macrophage-mediated platelet clearance and accelerates disease progression of immune thrombocytopenia (ITP). Reduced ERN1 expression and IRE1α activity are observed in monocytes from patients with ITP. Pharmacological inhibition of NR1D1 or lysosomal activity rescues thrombocytopenia. Together, these findings establish the IRE1α-NR1D1-lysosome axis as a therapeutically actionable pathway in phagocytosis-driven diseases.

> **中文摘要：**
> 巨噬细胞吞噬作用对于免疫稳态至关重要，但必须受到严格限制以防止病理性组织损伤。细胞应激通路如何维持吞噬稳态仍不完全清楚。本文中，我们发现吞噬作用选择性地激活巨噬细胞中的内质网应激传感器IRE1α，其作为溶酶体驱动的吞噬放大的负向调节因子发挥作用。利用髓系特异性IRE1α缺陷小鼠和药理学抑制手段，我们证明IRE1α RNase活性的丧失会通过不受控制的溶酶体生物发生导致过度吞噬。从机制上讲，被吞噬作用激活的IRE1α通过受调控的IRE1α依赖性衰变（RIDD）途径直接降解Nr1d1 mRNA，从而抑制NR1D1驱动的溶酶体扩增。破坏这一IRE1α-NR1D1轴会加剧巨噬细胞介导的血小板清除，并加速免疫性血小板减少症（ITP）的疾病进展。在ITP患者的单核细胞中观察到ERN1表达和IRE1α活性降低。药理学抑制NR1D1或溶酶体活性可挽救血小板减少症。总之，这些发现确立了IRE1α-NR1D1-溶酶体轴作为吞噬驱动疾病中一个可治疗的靶向通路。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在阐明内质网应激感应器IRE1α在巨噬细胞吞噬稳态中的调控作用及其在免疫性血小板减少症（ITP）中的病理意义。研究者综合运用了髓系特异性基因敲除小鼠、药理学干预及患者样本分析，揭示了吞噬作用通过激活IRE1α的RNase活性，降解Nr1d1 mRNA以限制溶酶体生物发生，从而负反馈调控吞噬活性的新机制。其创新性在于首次将IRE1α的RIDD功能与溶酶体通路及ITP的病理过程直接联系起来，并提出了靶向NR1D1或溶酶体的治疗新策略。局限性在于研究主要聚焦于ITP模型，该轴在其他吞噬相关疾病中的普适性及详细的体内药效学有待进一步验证。

---

## 44. 来那度胺治疗多发性骨髓瘤后，IDH2克隆性造血与IKAROS缺失协同作用驱动一种B-ALL亚型的发生

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41824395)
**期刊：** Blood
**PMID：** 41824395
**DOI：** 10.1182/blood.2025031047

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** IDH2 Clonal Hematopoiesis and IKAROS Loss Cooperate in a B-ALL Subtype after Lenalidomide Therapy for Multiple Myeloma.

> **英文摘要：**
> Lenalidomide, a maintenance treatment in multiple myeloma first-line therapy, increases the risk of secondary malignancies, including B-cell precursor acute lymphoblastic leukemia (B‑ALL). We present a comprehensive molecular characterization of 57 patients with lenalidomide-associated B-ALL (LenB-ALL), revealing three mutational subgroups: (1) TP53mt (30%), (2) IDH2mt (p.R140Q) (23%) and (3) other, including NRAS/KRASmt. Remarkably, IDH2 R140Q mutations were highly enriched in LenB-ALL compared to primary B-ALL (p<0.001). Furthermore, IKZF1 intragenic deletions - often subclonal and likely RAG-mediated - were observed in 54% (7/13) of IDH2mt LenB-ALL cases. IDH2 mutations were not restricted to the leukemic clone: they persisted during MRD-negative remission and were identified in lymphoid as well as myeloid cell populations using fluorescence-activated cell sorting and single-cell RNA sequencing. This indicates a preleukemic origin of the IDH2 mutation within the context of clonal hematopoiesis. Transcriptomic and DNA methylation analyses revealed a distinct gene expression profile and a DNA hypermethylation phenotype in IDH2mt LenB-ALL, including IDH2mt-specific as well as lenalidomide-associated features. We propose that lenalidomide promotes expansion of IDH2-mutated clonal hematopoiesis and, via IKAROS downregulation, induces a maturation arrest at the B-cell precursor stage. Subsequent genetic or epigenetic alterations render leukemogenesis independent of ongoing lenalidomide exposure. Altogether, these data define IDH2mt B-ALL as a distinct molecular subtype that is markedly overrepresented after lenalidomide treatment and highlight clonal hematopoiesis as a key contributing factor in the development of LenB-ALL.

> **中文摘要：**
> 来那度胺是多发性骨髓瘤一线治疗中的维持疗法，会增加继发性恶性肿瘤的风险，包括B细胞前体急性淋巴细胞白血病（B-ALL）。我们对57例来那度胺相关B-ALL（LenB-ALL）患者进行了全面的分子特征分析，揭示了三个突变亚组：（1）TP53突变（30%），（2）IDH2突变（p.R140Q）（23%）和（3）其他，包括NRAS/KRAS突变。值得注意的是，与原发性B-ALL相比，IDH2 R140Q突变在LenB-ALL中高度富集（p<0.001）。此外，在54%（7/13）的IDH2突变型LenB-ALL病例中观察到IKZF1基因内缺失——这些缺失通常是亚克隆性的，且可能由RAG介导。IDH2突变并不局限于白血病克隆：它们在微小残留病灶阴性的缓解期持续存在，并通过流式细胞分选和单细胞RNA测序在淋巴系和髓系细胞群中被鉴定出来。这表明IDH2突变起源于克隆性造血背景下的白血病前阶段。转录组学和DNA甲基化分析揭示了IDH2突变型LenB-ALL具有独特的基因表达谱和DNA高甲基化表型，包括IDH2突变特异性特征以及来那度胺相关特征。我们提出，来那度胺促进了IDH2突变克隆性造血的扩增，并通过下调IKAROS，诱导B细胞前体阶段发生成熟阻滞。随后的遗传或表观遗传改变使得白血病发生不再依赖于持续的来那度胺暴露。总而言之，这些数据将IDH2突变型B-ALL定义为一个独特的分子亚型，该亚型在来那度胺治疗后显著高发，并强调了克隆性造血是LenB-ALL发生的关键促成因素。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在阐明来那度胺治疗后继发B-ALL（LenB-ALL）的分子机制。通过对57例患者进行多组学分析，研究者发现IDH2突变型LenB-ALL是一个显著富集的独特亚型，其IDH2突变起源于白血病前的克隆性造血，并常与亚克隆性、RAG介导的IKZF1缺失协同作用。研究创新性地提出了来那度胺通过促进IDH2突变克隆扩增和下调IKAROS导致B细胞成熟阻滞，进而驱动白血病的两阶段模型，强调了克隆性造血在治疗相关白血病中的核心作用。局限性在于样本量相对有限，且对来那度胺如何特异性促进IDH2突变克隆扩增的具体机制仍需进一步实验验证。

---

## 45. 放疗治疗惰性原发性皮肤B细胞淋巴瘤：一项国际淋巴瘤放射肿瘤学组（ILROG）多中心分析。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41824381)
**期刊：** Blood
**PMID：** 41824381
**DOI：** 10.1182/blood.2025032050

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Radiotherapy for indolent primary cutaneous B-cell lymphoma: an international multicenter ILROG analysis.

> **英文摘要：**
> Radiotherapy is an established treatment for low-grade primary cutaneous B-cell lymphoma. Recommendations on its use differ internationally, which prompted our group to conduct the present analysis. Twenty-two institutions participated in this international study. Patient eligibility required a diagnosis of limited (T1/T2) primary cutaneous marginal zone or follicle center lymphoma treated with radiotherapy between 1995 and 2023. Data were collected retrospectively until February 2024 in the framework of the International Lymphoma Radiation Oncology Group. Overall, 535 patients were analyzed. Predominant locations were the head (40%) and trunk (36%). Radiotherapy had a median dose of 24 Gy in fractions of 2 Gy. Complete responses were seen in 91% at a median time of 3.6 months following radiotherapy. There was no statistically significant difference between treatments ≤4 Gy or >4 Gy for complete or overall response rates (p=0.077 and p=0.056). However, there was an inferior duration of local control with ≤4 Gy (5-year local control 73% ± 12% vs. 96% ± 2%; p<0.001). Radiation dose was the main prognostic factor in the univariate and multivariate Cox analysis; however, higher doses did not translate into an overall survival benefit. Toxicities rarely exceeded grade 2 but were more frequent in the >4 Gy group. Radiotherapy remains an effective treatment option for indolent skin lymphoma with low toxicities. High response rates are observed with low doses ≤4 Gy. In comparison to conventional doses, these treatments have a shorter duration of local control but a favorable toxicity profile.

> **中文摘要：**
> 放疗是治疗低级别原发性皮肤B细胞淋巴瘤的一种既定方法。国际上对其使用的建议存在差异，这促使我们团队进行了本次分析。本研究有22家机构参与。患者入选标准为1995年至2023年间接受放疗治疗的局限性（T1/T2期）原发性皮肤边缘区淋巴瘤或滤泡中心淋巴瘤。数据在国际淋巴瘤放射肿瘤学组框架下进行回顾性收集，截至2024年2月。总共分析了535名患者。主要发病部位为头部（40%）和躯干（36%）。放疗中位剂量为24 Gy，分割剂量为2 Gy。91%的患者在放疗后中位时间3.6个月时达到完全缓解。对于完全缓解率或总缓解率，≤4 Gy与>4 Gy的治疗方案之间无统计学显著差异（p=0.077和p=0.056）。然而，≤4 Gy组的局部控制持续时间较差（5年局部控制率 73% ± 12% vs. 96% ± 2%；p<0.001）。在单变量和多变量Cox分析中，放疗剂量是主要的预后因素；然而，更高的剂量并未转化为总生存获益。毒性反应很少超过2级，但在>4 Gy组中更常见。放疗仍然是治疗惰性皮肤淋巴瘤的有效选择，且毒性较低。使用≤4 Gy的低剂量可观察到高缓解率。与传统剂量相比，这些治疗的局部控制持续时间较短，但具有更优的毒性特征。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在通过国际多中心回顾性分析，澄清放疗在惰性原发性皮肤B细胞淋巴瘤治疗中的剂量效应关系。核心发现是，低剂量（≤4 Gy）放疗可获得高缓解率且毒性谱更优，但其局部控制持续时间显著短于常规剂量（>4 Gy），尽管剂量高低并不影响总生存。该研究为临床实践中个体化剂量选择提供了重要证据，其创新性在于基于大样本数据明确了低剂量放疗的疗效与局限性。局限性在于其回顾性设计，可能存在选择偏倚，且未能明确界定最优的低剂量分割方案。

---

## 47. 设计锰铂双金属纳米酶用于级联酶疗法与增强型放射免疫治疗。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41821152)
**期刊：** Advanced science (Weinheim, Baden-Wurttemberg, Germany)
**PMID：** 41821152
**DOI：** 10.1002/advs.202519300

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Engineering MnPt Bimetallic Nanozymes for Cascade Enzymatic Therapy and Enhanced Radio-Immunotherapy.

> **英文摘要：**
> The immunosuppressive tumor microenvironment (TME) promotes resistance to radiation therapy, substantially limiting the efficacy of radioimmunotherapy. Here, we report a hyaluronic acid (HA)-coated manganese-platinum (MnPt) bimetallic nanozyme (HD@MnO) that integrates enzymatic cascade initiation with cGAS-STING pathway activation to facilitate radioimmunotherapy for breast cancer treatment. The HD@MnO features a cationic MnO core sequentially modified with HA and cisplatin, enabling CD44-targeted delivery and improved biocompatibility. Leveraging the reversible valence cycling of Mn and Pt in the TME, HD@MnO offers multienzyme-like activity, which collectively enhances HO utilization, depletes glutathione, and promotes O generation. These cascade reactions combined with radiotherapy effectively trigger bursts of ROS production, disrupt redox homeostasis, and induce immunogenic cell death. Concurrently, released Mn  activates the cGAS-STING pathway, thereby boosting innate immunity. The combination of these effects promotes dendritic cell maturation and increases CD8 T cell infiltration, thereby establishing a radiotherapy-immune mutual amplification loop. Both in vitro and in vivo experiments demonstrated that HD@MnO markedly eliminates primary tumors and suppresses metastatic tumors by overcoming radioresistance and eliciting potent systemic antitumor immunity. Overall, this approach offers a promising strategy for addressing the conventional limitations of radioimmunotherapy.

> **中文摘要：**
> 免疫抑制性肿瘤微环境（TME）会促进对放射治疗的抵抗，从而极大地限制了放射免疫治疗的疗效。在此，我们报道了一种透明质酸（HA）包被的锰-铂（MnPt）双金属纳米酶（HD@MnO），它整合了级联酶反应启动与cGAS-STING通路激活，以促进乳腺癌治疗的放射免疫治疗。HD@MnO具有一个阳离子MnO核心，该核心依次被HA和顺铂修饰，从而实现了CD44靶向递送并提高了生物相容性。利用Mn和Pt在TME中的可逆价态循环，HD@MnO提供了多种类酶活性，这些活性共同增强了H₂O₂的利用、消耗了谷胱甘肽并促进了O₂的生成。这些级联反应与放射治疗相结合，有效触发了活性氧（ROS）的爆发式产生，破坏了氧化还原稳态，并诱导了免疫原性细胞死亡。同时，释放的Mn²⁺激活了cGAS-STING通路，从而增强了先天免疫。这些效应的结合促进了树突状细胞的成熟并增加了CD8⁺ T细胞的浸润，从而建立了一个放射治疗-免疫相互放大的循环。体外和体内实验均表明，HD@MnO通过克服放射抵抗并引发强大的全身性抗肿瘤免疫，显著消除了原发性肿瘤并抑制了转移性肿瘤。总体而言，该方法为解决放射免疫治疗的传统局限性提供了一个有前景的策略。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在克服肿瘤微环境（TME）免疫抑制导致的放射免疫治疗抵抗。其核心创新在于设计了一种多功能双金属纳米酶HD@MnO，它巧妙地将级联催化反应（增强氧化应激、破坏氧化还原稳态）与cGAS-STING通路激活相结合，从而在放射治疗基础上，协同诱导免疫原性细胞死亡并激活先天免疫，最终构建了“放疗-免疫”相互放大的正向循环。实验结果表明，该策略能有效消除原发灶并抑制转移，为增强放射免疫治疗疗效提供了新思路。然而，摘要未提及该纳米系统的长期生物安全性、大规模生产工艺及潜在的脱靶效应，这些是未来临床转化前需深入评估的关键问题。

## 50. 选择性自噬在癌症中的多功能性：分子基础、影响及临床前景。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41820985)
**期刊：** Molecular cancer
**PMID：** 41820985
**DOI：** 10.1186/s12943-026-02615-8

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** The multifaceted functions of selective autophagy in cancer: molecular basis, consequences, and clinical prospects.

> **英文摘要：**
> Selective autophagy is a critical cellular process in eukaryotic cells, characterized by the targeted degradation of specific organelles and proteins. This intricate mechanism plays a vital role in maintaining cellular homeostasis and has significant implications in the pathogenesis and progression of various diseases, notably cancer. Recent studies have highlighted the dual role of selective autophagy in cancer, acting both as a suppressor in the early stages and potentially facilitating progression in later stages. The complexity of selective autophagy, particularly in the context of oncogenesis, presents unique challenges. This review focuses on the molecular mechanisms underlying selective autophagy, its impact on cancer development and progression, and the challenges in leveraging this process for therapeutic interventions. We discuss the interplay between autophagy and cancer, examining how alterations in autophagic pathways contribute to tumorigenesis and the resistance of cancer cells to therapy. Additionally, we explore the potential of targeting selective autophagy pathways as a novel approach in cancer treatment, considering the challenges and prospects of such strategies.

> **中文摘要：**
> 选择性自噬是真核细胞中一个关键的细胞过程，其特点是特异性降解特定的细胞器和蛋白质。这一复杂机制在维持细胞稳态中起着至关重要的作用，并对多种疾病（尤其是癌症）的发病机制和进展具有重要影响。最近的研究强调了选择性自噬在癌症中的双重作用，既在早期阶段充当抑制因子，又可能在后期阶段促进进展。选择性自噬的复杂性，特别是在肿瘤发生的背景下，带来了独特的挑战。本综述重点探讨选择性自噬的分子机制、其对癌症发生和进展的影响，以及利用这一过程进行治疗干预所面临的挑战。我们讨论了自噬与癌症之间的相互作用，研究了自噬通路的变化如何促进肿瘤发生以及癌细胞对治疗的抵抗。此外，考虑到此类策略的挑战和前景，我们探索了靶向选择性自噬通路作为癌症治疗新方法的潜力。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本文是一篇综述，旨在系统阐述选择性自噬在癌症中的复杂作用。其核心目的是梳理该过程的分子基础，分析其对癌症发生发展的双重影响，并评估其作为治疗靶点的临床前景。方法上，文章综合了近期研究，重点剖析了自噬通路改变与肿瘤发生、治疗抵抗之间的相互作用。文章的创新性在于强调了选择性自噬在癌症不同阶段的动态角色，并前瞻性地探讨了靶向干预的潜力。局限性在于作为一篇综述，其结论依赖于现有研究的整合，对于如何精确调控其双重功能以实现有效治疗，仍面临巨大挑战，需要更多机制研究和临床验证。

## 52. 用于动态人工智能评估的临床环境模拟器

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41820673)
**期刊：** Nature medicine
**PMID：** 41820673
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41591-026-04252-6

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** A clinical environment simulator for dynamic AI evaluation.

> **英文摘要：**
> Clinical evaluation of large language models (LLMs) currently relies on static datasets and isolated scenarios that fail to capture the cascading effects of healthcare decisions. We propose the Clinical Environment Simulator (CES), a framework that evaluates clinical LLMs within digital hospital environments where every decision dynamically alters future states. The CES would use a parallel simulation architecture: a 'hospital engine' that tracks bed availability, staff workloads and equipment status in real time, and a 'patient engine' that simulates disease progression and treatment responses based on LLM interventions. Unlike current benchmarks, the CES framework requires clinical LLMs to execute decisions through realistic electronic health record interfaces, while managing trade-offs between individual patient optimization and system-wide efficiency. The CES enables three critical evaluations absent from current benchmarks: temporal reasoning under evolving constraints, where delayed diagnostics can lead to patient deterioration; resource-aware decision-making, where aggressive workups for one patient may exhaust capacity needed by others; and operational resilience, through adversarial testing with simultaneous emergencies and system failures. By scoring LLM performance on both clinical outcomes and operational metrics, the CES represents a shift toward evaluating clinical LLMs as a dynamic and integrated component of healthcare delivery systems.

> **中文摘要：**
> 目前，大型语言模型（LLMs）的临床评估依赖于静态数据集和孤立场景，无法捕捉医疗决策的连锁效应。我们提出了临床环境模拟器（CES），这是一个在数字化医院环境中评估临床LLMs的框架，其中每个决策都会动态改变未来状态。CES将采用并行模拟架构：一个实时跟踪床位可用性、医护人员工作量和设备状态的“医院引擎”，以及一个基于LLM干预措施模拟疾病进展和治疗反应的“患者引擎”。与现有基准不同，CES框架要求临床LLMs通过逼真的电子健康记录界面执行决策，同时管理个体患者优化与系统整体效率之间的权衡。CES实现了当前基准中缺失的三项关键评估：在不断变化的约束下进行时序推理（延迟诊断可能导致患者病情恶化）；资源感知决策（对一名患者的积极检查可能耗尽其他患者所需的资源）；以及通过模拟同时发生的紧急情况和系统故障进行对抗性测试，以评估运行韧性。通过结合临床结果和运行指标对LLM性能进行评分，CES代表了一种转变，即将临床LLMs作为医疗服务提供系统中动态且集成的组成部分进行评估。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

该研究旨在解决当前临床大语言模型（LLM）评估方法的局限性，提出了一种创新的临床环境模拟器（CES）框架。其核心方法是通过构建包含“医院引擎”和“患者引擎”的并行数字模拟环境，动态评估LLM决策在资源约束和时序变化下的真实影响。该框架的创新性在于首次将临床决策评估从静态、孤立的问答场景，拓展到动态、交互、资源敏感的复杂系统层面，能够评估时序推理、资源权衡和运行韧性等关键能力。然而，其局限性在于该框架目前仍是一个概念性提案，其模拟环境的保真度、验证方法以及对现实医疗流程的覆盖程度，尚需后续实证研究的检验和细化。

## 54. SHP1蛋白上的一个可靶向氧化还原开关调控巨噬细胞炎症反应。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41820548)
**期刊：** Nature chemical biology
**PMID：** 41820548
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41589-026-02163-8

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** A druggable redox switch on SHP1 controls macrophage inflammation.

> **英文摘要：**
> Immunological proteins are major disease targets, yet most remain undrugged. Post-translational redox modification of cysteine residues has emerged as an important mode of immune cell regulation, particularly in macrophage cytokine responses. Here we develop a strategy for systematic discovery and small-molecule functionalization of redox-regulated cysteines on immunological proteins. Using deep redox proteomics, we annotate 788 in vivo redox-regulated cysteines across diverse immune-relevant protein domains. We demonstrate how these sites enable cysteine-directed pharmacology through discovery of a novel cysteine activation site on the immune regulator SHP1. Targeting C102, we develop a highly selective covalent agonist, SCA, which binds the N-SH2 domain to relieve autoinhibition and activate SHP1. In mouse and human macrophages, SCA selectively engages SHP1 C102, antagonizing interleukin-1 receptor-associated kinase signaling and lipopolysaccharide-induced proinflammatory cytokine production. Together, this work identifies a druggable cysteine redox switch controlling macrophage cytokine responses and provides a compendium of redox-regulated sites for therapeutic development.

> **中文摘要：**
> 免疫蛋白是主要的疾病靶点，但大多数仍未被药物靶向。半胱氨酸残基的翻译后氧化还原修饰已成为免疫细胞调控的重要模式，尤其是在巨噬细胞细胞因子反应中。在此，我们开发了一种策略，用于系统性地发现免疫蛋白上受氧化还原调控的半胱氨酸并实现其小分子功能化。利用深度氧化还原蛋白质组学，我们注释了788个在体内受氧化还原调控的半胱氨酸位点，这些位点分布于多种免疫相关蛋白结构域中。我们通过发现免疫调节因子SHP1上一个新的半胱氨酸激活位点，展示了这些位点如何实现半胱氨酸导向的药理学。针对C102位点，我们开发了一种高选择性的共价激动剂SCA，它能结合N-SH2结构域，解除自抑制并激活SHP1。在小鼠和人类巨噬细胞中，SCA选择性作用于SHP1的C102位点，拮抗白细胞介素-1受体相关激酶信号通路，并抑制脂多糖诱导的促炎细胞因子产生。总之，这项工作发现了一个控制巨噬细胞细胞因子反应的可靶向半胱氨酸氧化还原开关，并提供了一个用于治疗开发的氧化还原调控位点汇编。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在通过系统发现免疫蛋白上的氧化还原调控半胱氨酸位点，为开发靶向性药物提供新策略。核心方法是结合深度氧化还原蛋白质组学与靶向性小分子设计，成功在免疫调节因子SHP1上鉴定出关键的C102位点，并开发出高选择性共价激动剂SCA。主要发现是证实了SCA通过激活SHP1，能够有效抑制巨噬细胞的促炎信号通路和细胞因子产生，从而揭示了一个全新的、可药物化的炎症调控机制。其创新性在于将蛋白质氧化还原修饰图谱与精准共价药物开发相结合，为免疫疾病治疗提供了新靶点和工具分子，但研究目前主要聚焦于巨噬细胞模型，其体内疗效和潜在脱靶效应仍需进一步验证。

## 55. 用于联合分析单细胞RNA与T细胞受体测序数据的多模态框架可预测T细胞对癌症免疫治疗的反应

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41820396)
**期刊：** Nature communications
**PMID：** 41820396
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41467-026-70505-0

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Multimodal framework for the joint analysis of single-cell RNA and T cell receptor sequencing data predicts T cell response to cancer immunotherapy.

> **英文摘要：**
> T cell states are prognostic in different cancer types. Recent technologies enable joint profiling of T cell RNA and T cell receptor (TCR) sequences at single-cell resolution. Here we present the TCR-RNA Integrating Model (TRIM), a multi-modal variational autoencoder framework that integrates RNA-TCR data and predicts T cell clonality and transcriptional states. TRIM learns a shared representation of the data conditioned on patient, tissue source, and treatment timepoint. We applied TRIM to three independent datasets that included T cells collected before and after checkpoint inhibitor treatment, sourced either from blood and tumor biopsies in patients with head and neck squamous cell carcinoma and colorectal cancer, or from tumor and adjacent tissue in a pan-cancer dataset. In all settings, TRIM accurately predicted intra-tumor T cell clonal expansion and transcriptional status based on T cells from blood or normal tissue before treatment, demonstrating its utility in modeling multimodal T cell data and predicting T cell response to treatment and disease progression.

> **中文摘要：**
> T细胞状态在不同癌症类型中具有预后价值。近期技术使得在单细胞分辨率下联合分析T细胞RNA与T细胞受体（TCR）序列成为可能。在此，我们提出了TCR-RNA整合模型（TRIM），这是一个整合RNA-TCR数据并预测T细胞克隆性与转录状态的多模态变分自编码器框架。TRIM学习了一个以患者、组织来源和治疗时间点为条件的共享数据表征。我们将TRIM应用于三个独立的数据集，这些数据集包含了在检查点抑制剂治疗前后收集的T细胞，来源包括头颈鳞状细胞癌和结直肠癌患者的血液与肿瘤活检样本，以及一个泛癌数据集中的肿瘤与邻近组织。在所有场景下，TRIM均能基于治疗前来自血液或正常组织的T细胞，准确预测肿瘤内T细胞的克隆扩增和转录状态，这证明了其在建模多模态T细胞数据以及预测T细胞对治疗和疾病进展反应方面的实用性。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在开发一个整合单细胞RNA与TCR测序数据的多模态分析框架，以预测T细胞对免疫治疗的反应。其核心创新在于提出了TRIM模型，这是一个基于变分自编码器的框架，能够整合多模态数据并学习受患者、组织和时间点条件约束的共享表征。研究发现，TRIM能够利用治疗前的血液或正常组织T细胞数据，准确预测治疗后肿瘤内T细胞的克隆扩增和转录状态，展示了其作为预测生物标志物工具的潜力。然而，其预测性能仍需在更大规模、前瞻性的临床队列中得到进一步验证，并且模型的可解释性及其对特定T细胞亚群预测的精确度是未来需要探索的方向。

## 56. ctDNA与肿瘤生物标志物在acelERA乳腺癌研究中预测giredestrant疗效的分析

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41820395)
**期刊：** Nature communications
**PMID：** 41820395
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41467-026-70335-0

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** ctDNA and tumor-based biomarkers of giredestrant response in acelERA breast cancer.

> **英文摘要：**
> Endocrine therapy (ET) resistance in estrogen receptor positive (ER+) advanced breast cancer is often linked to ESR1 mutations, yet responses to oral selective ER degraders vary within mutant subgroups. Through a biomarker analysis of acelERA Breast Cancer (NCT04576455), we show that tumor ER transcriptional activity as well as circulating tumor DNA (ctDNA) genomics and dynamics effectively stratify response to ET, including giredestrant. We find that following first-line therapy, the ctDNA genomic landscape is diverse and influenced by CDK4/6 inhibitor exposure. Despite this complexity, ER activity in ESR1-mutant tumors remains comparable to early breast cancer but is reduced in most non-mutant cases. This maintained ER activity is associated with giredestrant benefit. Furthermore, early ctDNA clearance identifies responding patients, and the combination of low ER activity and high ctDNA burden predicts rapid clinical progression. These findings provide a framework for personalizing future breast cancer therapies by integrating liquid biopsies with tissue-based signatures.

> **中文摘要：**
> 雌激素受体阳性（ER+）晚期乳腺癌的内分泌治疗（ET）耐药常与ESR1突变相关，但在突变亚组内，患者对口服选择性ER降解剂的反应存在差异。通过对acelERA乳腺癌研究（NCT04576455）的生物标志物分析，我们发现肿瘤ER转录活性以及循环肿瘤DNA（ctDNA）的基因组学特征和动态变化能有效分层预测包括giredestrant在内的ET疗效。我们发现，在一线治疗后，ctDNA基因组图谱呈现多样性，并受CDK4/6抑制剂暴露的影响。尽管存在这种复杂性，ESR1突变肿瘤中的ER活性仍与早期乳腺癌相当，但在大多数非突变病例中则有所降低。这种持续的ER活性与giredestrant的临床获益相关。此外，早期ctDNA清除可识别出有应答的患者，而低ER活性与高ctDNA负荷的组合则能预测快速的临床进展。这些发现为通过整合液体活检和组织特征来个性化未来乳腺癌治疗提供了一个框架。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在探索预测新型口服选择性ER降解剂giredestrant疗效的生物标志物。通过分析acelERA临床试验数据，创新性地整合了肿瘤组织ER转录活性和ctDNA基因组学/动力学特征。核心发现包括：ESR1突变肿瘤中ER活性得以维持并与giredestrant获益相关，早期ctDNA清除是疗效预测指标，而低ER活性与高ctDNA负荷的组合则提示不良预后。其创新性在于构建了一个结合液体活检（ctDNA）与组织特征（ER活性）的个性化治疗框架，为克服内分泌耐药提供了新思路。局限性在于分析基于特定临床试验的样本，其结论的普适性及在更广泛治疗线数中的验证仍需进一步研究。

## 57. VHL合成致死筛选揭示CBF-β是STING的负调控因子。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41820368)
**期刊：** Nature communications
**PMID：** 41820368
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41467-026-70517-w

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** VHL synthetic lethality screens uncover CBF-β as a negative regulator of STING.

> **英文摘要：**
> Clear cell renal cell carcinoma (ccRCC) represents the most common form of kidney cancer and is typified by biallelic inactivation of the von Hippel-Lindau (VHL) tumour suppressor gene. Here, we undertake genome-wide CRISPR/Cas9 screening to reveal synthetic lethal interactors of VHL, and uncover that loss of Core Binding Factor β (CBF-β) causes cell death in VHL-null ccRCC cell lines and impairs tumour establishment and growth in vivo. This synthetic relationship is independent of the elevated activity of hypoxia inducible factors (HIFs) in VHL-null cells, but does involve the RUNX transcription factors that are known binding partners of CBF-β. Mechanistically, CBF-β loss leads to upregulation of type I interferon signalling, and we uncover a direct inhibitory role for CBF-β at the STING locus controlling Interferon Stimulated Gene expression. Targeting CBF-β in kidney cancer both selectively induces tumour cell lethality and promotes activation of type I interferon signalling.

> **中文摘要：**
> 透明细胞肾细胞癌（ccRCC）是最常见的肾癌形式，其典型特征是von Hippel-Lindau（VHL）肿瘤抑制基因的双等位基因失活。本研究通过全基因组CRISPR/Cas9筛选来揭示VHL的合成致死相互作用因子，并发现核心结合因子β（CBF-β）的缺失会导致VHL缺失的ccRCC细胞系发生细胞死亡，并在体内损害肿瘤的形成和生长。这种合成致死关系不依赖于VHL缺失细胞中缺氧诱导因子（HIFs）活性的升高，但确实涉及已知的CBF-β结合伙伴RUNX转录因子。从机制上讲，CBF-β的缺失导致I型干扰素信号通路上调，并且我们发现CBF-β在控制干扰素刺激基因表达的STING基因位点具有直接的抑制作用。在肾癌中靶向CBF-β既能选择性诱导肿瘤细胞死亡，又能促进I型干扰素信号通路的激活。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在探索VHL缺失肾癌的潜在治疗靶点。研究者采用全基因组CRISPR/Cas9合成致死筛选，创新性地发现CBF-β是VHL缺失背景下的一个关键致死性靶点。其核心发现是，CBF-β缺失通过上调I型干扰素信号通路诱导癌细胞死亡，并首次揭示CBF-β直接抑制STING基因位点，这为理解肿瘤免疫调控提供了新机制。然而，研究主要基于细胞系和体内模型，其临床转化潜力及在更广泛肿瘤类型中的适用性仍需进一步验证。

---

## 58. 催化邻近蛋白质寡聚化：一种靶向WDR5的抗肿瘤策略

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41820364)
**期刊：** Nature communications
**PMID：** 41820364
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41467-026-70409-z

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Catalytic Proximal Protein Oligomerization as an Anti-Tumor Strategy Targeting WDR5.

> **英文摘要：**
> Inducing protein oligomerization holds therapeutic promise, yet identifying or rationally designing effective inducers remains challenging. In this study, we leverage nanopore technology to screen small molecules capable of modulating WD repeat domain 5 (WDR5) protein oligomerization and uncover a oligomerization mechanism which we term Catalytic Proximal Protein Oligomerization (CaPPO). Nanopore sensing enabled rapid identification of WZ-1, a selective WDR5 oligomerization inducer, from our in-house compound library. Biochemical and cryo-EM analyses reveal that WZ-1 binds the WBM site of WDR5 through its 2-aminothiazole moiety, reacts with Cys248 to form an intramolecular disulfide, and, through N-terminal tail-induced proximity of WDR5 molecules, triggers oligomerization via thio-disulfide exchange. Structure-activity relationship studies indicate that the disulfide motif within WZ-1 acts as a molecular scout initiating oligomerization. In cellular assays, WZ-1 exhibits potent anti-tumor activity by disrupting WDR5 interactions at both WIN and WBM sites, leading to transcriptional downregulation of target genes. Collectively, this work not only establishes a nanopore-based screening platform for identifying protein oligomerization inducers, but also validates CaPPO as a promising small-molecule design strategy for therapeutic development.

> **中文摘要：**
> 诱导蛋白质寡聚化具有治疗前景，但识别或合理设计有效的诱导剂仍然具有挑战性。在本研究中，我们利用纳米孔技术筛选能够调节WD重复结构域5（WDR5）蛋白质寡聚化的小分子，并揭示了一种我们称之为催化邻近蛋白质寡聚化（CaPPO）的机制。纳米孔传感技术使我们能够从内部化合物库中快速鉴定出WZ-1，一种选择性的WDR5寡聚化诱导剂。生化和冷冻电镜分析表明，WZ-1通过其2-氨基噻唑部分结合WDR5的WBM位点，与Cys248反应形成分子内二硫键，并通过N端尾部诱导的WDR5分子邻近性，通过硫醇-二硫键交换触发寡聚化。构效关系研究表明，WZ-1内部的二硫键基序充当了启动寡聚化的分子“侦察兵”。在细胞实验中，WZ-1通过破坏WDR5在WIN和WBM两个位点的相互作用，导致靶基因的转录下调，从而表现出强大的抗肿瘤活性。总之，这项工作不仅建立了一个基于纳米孔的筛选平台用于识别蛋白质寡聚化诱导剂，而且验证了CaPPO作为一种有前景的小分子设计策略用于治疗开发。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在开发一种靶向WDR5蛋白的抗肿瘤新策略。其核心创新在于结合纳米孔高通量筛选技术与结构生物学手段，发现并阐明了一种全新的小分子诱导蛋白质寡聚化机制——催化邻近蛋白质寡聚化（CaPPO）。研究不仅成功鉴定出先导化合物WZ-1，揭示了其通过共价修饰和硫醇-二硫键交换催化WDR5寡聚的分子细节，更在细胞层面验证了其通过双重破坏WDR5蛋白-蛋白相互作用而发挥抗肿瘤活性的有效性。这项工作为发现蛋白质寡聚化调节剂提供了强大的技术平台，并概念性验证了CaPPO这一原创性药物设计策略，但该策略的普适性及其在活体动物模型中的疗效与安全性仍有待进一步探索。

---

## 59. 内源性VEGF信号通路作为人类始发态多能性的守护者。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41820363)
**期刊：** Nature communications
**PMID：** 41820363
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41467-026-70526-9

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Endogenous VEGF signaling acts as a guardian of human primed pluripotency.

> **英文摘要：**
> The maintenance of human embryonic stem cell (hESC) self-renewal and pluripotency is governed by distinct signaling pathways, yet endogenous pluripotency-supporting pathways remain understudied despite extensive exogenous signaling research. Here, we identify a previously unrecognized role of endogenous VEGF signaling in sustaining primed hESC pluripotency. VEGF signaling is robustly activated in primed hESCs, quiescent in naïve cells, and inactivated upon differentiation. Strikingly, targeted VEGFR inhibition (pharmacological, soluble decoy receptors [sFLT1/sKDR], or CRISPR-mediated VEGFR1/2 knockout) in primed hESCs disrupts self-renewal and induces trophoblast-like differentiation. Mechanistically, VEGFR inhibition activates the BMP pathway and down-regulates NANOG, which directly binds and represses select BMP components and trophoblast lineage-specific genes. Functionally, BMP inhibition partially and NANOG overexpression substantially rescue the phenotype induced by VEGF signaling ablation. Collectively, our work uncovers a pivotal VEGF-dependent network maintaining primed pluripotency, providing valuable insights into integrated pluripotency and lineage regulation by signaling cascades and transcription factors.

> **中文摘要：**
> 人类胚胎干细胞（hESC）的自我更新和多能性维持受不同信号通路调控，然而尽管对外源性信号传导进行了广泛研究，内源性支持多能性的通路仍未得到充分探索。在此，我们揭示了内源性VEGF信号通路在维持始发态hESC多能性中一个先前未被认识的作用。VEGF信号在始发态hESC中被强烈激活，在初始态细胞中处于静息状态，并在分化时失活。引人注目的是，在始发态hESC中靶向抑制VEGFR（药理学抑制、可溶性诱饵受体[sFLT1/sKDR]或CRISPR介导的VEGFR1/2敲除）会破坏其自我更新并诱导滋养层样分化。从机制上讲，VEGFR抑制会激活BMP通路并下调NANOG，而NANOG直接结合并抑制特定的BMP组分和滋养层谱系特异性基因。在功能上，抑制BMP可部分挽救，而过表达NANOG则可显著挽救由VEGF信号消除诱导的表型。总之，我们的工作揭示了一个维持始发态多能性的关键VEGF依赖性网络，为理解信号级联和转录因子如何整合调控多能性和谱系分化提供了有价值的见解。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在探索维持人胚胎干细胞始发态多能性的内源性信号通路，聚焦于VEGF信号。研究通过药理学、可溶性受体及CRISPR基因编辑等多种方法抑制VEGFR，并结合机制探索与功能挽救实验，系统揭示了内源性VEGF信号通过抑制BMP通路和维持NANOG表达来防止滋养层分化的新作用。其创新性在于首次将VEGF信号确立为始发态多能性的关键内源性守护者，并阐明了其与BMP/NANOG的调控网络，深化了对多能性稳态的理解。局限性在于研究主要基于体外细胞模型，其在体内发育环境中的生理相关性及在更广泛多能性状态（如初始态）中的作用仍需进一步验证。

---

## 60. 导电聚合物稳定的纳米酶通过抑制铁积累和脂质过氧化缓解脓毒症诱导的心肌损伤。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41820358)
**期刊：** Nature communications
**PMID：** 41820358
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41467-026-70385-4

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Conducting polymer-stabilized nanozymes alleviate sepsis-induced myocardial injury by inhibiting iron accumulation and lipid peroxidation.

> **英文摘要：**
> Septic cardiomyopathy (SC) is a severe complication of sepsis that significantly increases patient mortality. The onset of SC is associated with excessive reactive oxygen species (ROS), leading to increased oxidative stress and iron accumulation. Herein, we develop a library of conductive polypyrrole-polythiophene copolymer (PPy-co-PTh)-stabilized nanozymes by coordinating different metal ions within the copolymer framework. From this library, we identify a PPy-co-PTh stabilized ruthenium-based nanozyme (Ruzyme), which exhibits significant catalase- and superoxide dismutase-like activity, as well as nitrogen radical scavenging capability. Modifying the conductive interface significantly improves the catalytic activity and stability of the Ruzyme by lowering the catalytic energy barrier, reducing excessive oxidation caused by ROS, and facilitating the continuous decomposition of ROS. To achieve precise targeted delivery to myocardial mitochondria, (5-carboxypentyl) triphenyl phosphonium bromide (TPP-COOH) and a cardiac-targeting peptide (CTP) are conjugated onto the surface of the Ruzyme. In vitro, the stabilized nanozymes effectively scavenge ROS, reduce iron accumulation, and inhibit iron-dependent cell death, thereby lowering lipid peroxidation. In male SC mice, they improve cardiac function, demonstrating therapeutic benefits. Given the growing interest in nanozymes for cardiovascular diseases, this study provides a potential foundation for the development of therapeutic agents for severe cardiomyopathy and related conditions.

> **中文摘要：**
> 脓毒性心肌病（SC）是脓毒症的一种严重并发症，显著增加患者死亡率。SC的发生与过量的活性氧（ROS）有关，导致氧化应激增加和铁积累。在此，我们通过在共聚物框架内配位不同的金属离子，开发了一个导电聚吡咯-聚噻吩共聚物（PPy-co-PTh）稳定的纳米酶库。从这个库中，我们鉴定出一种PPy-co-PTh稳定的钌基纳米酶（Ruzyme），它表现出显著的类过氧化氢酶和超氧化物歧化酶活性，以及氮自由基清除能力。修饰导电界面通过降低催化能垒、减少ROS引起的过度氧化并促进ROS的持续分解，显著提高了Ruzyme的催化活性和稳定性。为了实现向心肌线粒体的精确靶向递送，将（5-羧戊基）三苯基溴化鏻（TPP-COOH）和心脏靶向肽（CTP）偶联到Ruzyme表面。在体外，稳定的纳米酶能有效清除ROS、减少铁积累并抑制铁依赖性细胞死亡，从而降低脂质过氧化。在雄性SC小鼠模型中，它们改善了心脏功能，显示出治疗益处。鉴于纳米酶在心血管疾病中的应用日益受到关注，本研究为开发针对严重心肌病及相关疾病的治疗药物提供了潜在基础。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在开发一种新型纳米酶疗法，以应对脓毒症心肌病中由活性氧和铁积累驱动的病理过程。其核心创新在于构建了导电聚合物稳定的纳米酶库，并从中筛选出具有多重抗氧化活性的钌基纳米酶，再通过靶向分子修饰实现心肌线粒体的精准递送。研究发现该纳米酶能有效清除自由基、减少铁死亡和脂质过氧化，并在动物模型中改善心功能，为心血管疾病的纳米酶治疗提供了新策略。局限性在于研究目前主要基于雄性小鼠模型，未来需验证其在更广泛模型中的疗效与安全性，并探索其临床转化的可行性。

## 62. 通过全基因组关联研究和胸腺瘤多组学分析阐明日本人群重症肌无力的遗传背景。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41820352)
**期刊：** Nature communications
**PMID：** 41820352
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41467-026-70376-5

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Elucidating genetic backgrounds of myasthenia gravis in Japanese by genome-wide association studies and multi-omics analyses of thymoma.

> **英文摘要：**
> Myasthenia gravis (MG) is an autoimmune disorder characterized by impaired neuromuscular transmission and motor symptoms. Its genetic background remains unclear, particularly beyond specific subtypes reported in European populations. Here, we perform a genome-wide association study (GWAS) of 1,434 MG cases covering all disease subtypes and 42,913 controls of Japanese, which newly identify the TERT locus (odds ratio [OR] = 1.31, P = 1.7×10). Subtype-stratified GWASs show stronger signals for generalized MG (gMG; OR = 1.38, P = 1.6×10), anti AChR antibody-positive gMG (g-AChR-Ab(+)MG; OR= 1.49, P = 2.1×10), and thymoma-associated gMG (g-TAMG; OR = 1.92, P = 1.1×10). Fine-mapping of the major histocompatibility complex region reveal distinct associations of HLA-DRB1 with late onset gMG (g-LOMG) and HLA-A with early onset gMG (g-EOMG). The MG risk TERT lead variant rs2736099 is associated with poor treatment response, especially in g-AChR-Ab(+)MG and g-EOMG (P < 0.0042). The biobank-based phenome-wide association study identify pleiotropic effects on lung cancer, hematological traits, and telomere length. Single cell transcriptomics and immunohistochemistry identified immature lymphocyte-specific TERT expression in thymoma specimens. Full-length transcriptomics reveal allele-specific decreasing effect of rs2736099-A on TERT expression. Our study unveils genetics of MG distinctly across disease subtypes, and involvement of TERT in its pathogenesis.

> **中文摘要：**
> 重症肌无力（MG）是一种以神经肌肉传递受损和运动症状为特征的自身免疫性疾病。其遗传背景尚不清楚，特别是在欧洲人群已报道的特定亚型之外。本研究对1434例涵盖所有疾病亚型的日本MG患者和42913例对照进行了全基因组关联研究（GWAS），新发现了TERT基因座（比值比[OR] = 1.31，P = 1.7×10）。亚型分层GWAS显示，在全身型MG（gMG；OR = 1.38，P = 1.6×10）、抗乙酰胆碱受体抗体阳性gMG（g-AChR-Ab(+)MG；OR= 1.49，P = 2.1×10）和胸腺瘤相关gMG（g-TAMG；OR = 1.92，P = 1.1×10）中信号更强。对主要组织相容性复合体区域的精细定位揭示了HLA-DRB1与晚发型gMG（g-LOMG）、HLA-A与早发型gMG（g-EOMG）的不同关联。MG风险相关的TERT先导变异rs2736099与较差的治疗反应相关，尤其是在g-AChR-Ab(+)MG和g-EOMG中（P < 0.0042）。基于生物样本库的表型组全关联研究发现了其对肺癌、血液学特征和端粒长度的多效性影响。单细胞转录组学和免疫组织化学在胸腺瘤标本中发现了未成熟淋巴细胞特异性的TERT表达。全长转录组学揭示了rs2736099-A等位基因对TERT表达的等位基因特异性降低效应。我们的研究揭示了MG遗传学在不同疾病亚型间的差异，以及TERT在其发病机制中的作用。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在通过大规模GWAS和多组学分析，系统阐明日本人群重症肌无力（MG）的遗传背景。核心方法是整合人群队列GWAS、亚型分层分析、HLA区域精细定位、表型组关联分析以及胸腺瘤的单细胞和全长转录组学，实现了从遗传关联到功能机制的探索。主要发现包括：新鉴定出TERT基因座为MG的跨亚型风险位点，揭示了其在胸腺瘤未成熟淋巴细胞中的特异性表达及等位基因特异性调控作用；明确了HLA等位基因与不同发病年龄亚型的特异性关联；并将TERT风险变异与临床治疗反应不良联系起来。创新性在于首次在非欧洲人群中对MG进行全面的遗传剖析，并利用多组学手段将TERT位点的遗传信号与胸腺瘤微环境及临床表型深度关联，为理解MG异质性和开发靶向策略提供了新见解。局限性可能在于样本量虽大但集中于日本人群，结论的普适性需在其他族群中验证，且功能机制研究主要基于胸腺瘤组织，对非胸腺瘤型MG的TERT作用路径阐述相对间接。

## 63. 撤稿说明：基于上转换纳米颗粒的免疫装置通过近红外光介导空间选择性触发抗肿瘤免疫。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41820345)
**期刊：** Nature communications
**PMID：** 41820345
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41467-026-70557-2

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Retraction Note: NIR-light-mediated spatially selective triggering of anti-tumor immunity via upconversion nanoparticle-based immunodevices.

> **英文摘要：**
> No abstract available.

> **中文摘要：**
> 无摘要。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

这是一篇撤稿说明，而非原始研究论文。原研究旨在开发一种创新的肿瘤免疫治疗策略，其核心是利用上转换纳米颗粒将穿透性强的近红外光转换为特定波长的光，从而在空间上精确激活免疫装置，以触发局部抗肿瘤免疫反应。该方法理论上具有非侵入性、高时空选择性的优势。然而，文章已被撤回，表明原始研究可能存在数据可靠性、实验可重复性或学术诚信方面的重大问题，其报告的创新性和结论需谨慎对待，不再作为有效科学依据。

## 64. 用于食管动力模拟的软体机器人仿生台式模型。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41820339)
**期刊：** Nature communications
**PMID：** 41820339
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41467-026-70260-2

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** A Soft-Robotic Biomimetic Benchtop Model for Esophageal Motility Simulation.

> **英文摘要：**
> Large animal models, while valuable, are expensive, time-consuming, and limited to discrete interventional or terminal timepoints, while existing benchtop models do not offer an accurate representation of the esophageal environment. Moreover, current pre-clinical models cannot effectively simulate swallowing dysfunction (dysphagia), restricting progress in understanding motility disorders like achalasia and hindering evidence-based dietary recommendations. In response, we present RoboGullet, a biomimetic soft-robotic model with independent localized longitudinal and circumferential muscle actuation, enabling, for the first time, simulation of both normal and diseased esophageal motility. We further enhance realism with a biohybrid variant, RoboGullet + , incorporating porcine esophageal mucosa/submucosa. We demonstrate this platform's versatility through three key applications: assessing stent migration, simulating achalasia I-III within clinical diagnostic criteria, and analyzing bolus swallowing. Our findings reveal that: (1) stent migration increases over fivefold when incorporating longitudinal muscle movement versus isolated circumferential; (2) using a viscous non-Newtonian bolus improves high-resolution manometry diagnostic sensitivity of Achalasia III through increasing the Distal Latency diagnostic metric by 20.83%; and (3) stirring Greek-style yoghurt (common non-Newtonian dietary recommendation) significantly improves bolus transit versus unstirred for Achalasia Types I-II patients. This establishes RoboGullet+ as a powerful translational tool, advancing our understanding of esophageal motility and its therapeutic interventions.

> **中文摘要：**
> 大型动物模型虽然有价值，但昂贵、耗时，且仅限于离散的干预或终末时间点，而现有的台式模型无法准确呈现食管环境。此外，当前的临床前模型无法有效模拟吞咽功能障碍（吞咽困难），限制了对贲门失弛缓症等动力障碍的理解进展，并阻碍了基于证据的饮食建议。为此，我们提出了RoboGullet，一种具有独立局部纵向和环向肌肉驱动的仿生软体机器人模型，首次实现了对正常和病变食管动力的模拟。我们通过引入猪食管黏膜/黏膜下层，进一步开发了生物混合变体RoboGullet+，以增强其真实性。我们通过三个关键应用展示了该平台的通用性：评估支架移位、在临床诊断标准内模拟贲门失弛缓症I-III型，以及分析食团吞咽。我们的研究结果表明：（1）与仅模拟环向运动相比，加入纵向肌肉运动时，支架移位增加了五倍以上；（2）使用粘性非牛顿食团，通过将远端潜伏期诊断指标提高20.83%，提高了高分辨率测压对贲门失弛缓症III型的诊断敏感性；（3）对于贲门失弛缓症I-II型患者，搅拌希腊式酸奶（常见的非牛顿饮食建议）相比未搅拌状态能显著改善食团通过。这确立了RoboGullet+作为一种强大的转化工具，增进了我们对食管动力及其治疗干预的理解。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在开发一种创新的仿生软体机器人平台（RoboGullet/RoboGullet+），以克服现有食管动力研究模型的局限性。其核心创新在于通过独立控制纵向与环向肌肉驱动，首次在台式模型中实现了对正常及病理状态（如贲门失弛缓症）食管动力学的精确模拟，并引入生物组织以增强真实性。研究发现强调了纵向肌肉运动对支架移位的显著影响，以及非牛顿食团特性在改善诊断敏感性和患者食团转运中的关键作用，为临床诊疗和器械评估提供了新见解。该模型作为强大的转化研究工具，潜力巨大，但其生物复杂性（如神经调控）的模拟程度及其发现向人体直接外推的有效性，仍需进一步验证。

---

## 65. 新一代KRAS G12C抑制剂olomorasib在KRAS G12C突变晚期实体瘤中的泛瘤种活性：一项首次人体研究。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41820335)
**期刊：** Nature communications
**PMID：** 41820335
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41467-026-69943-7

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Pan-tumor activity of olomorasib, a next-generation KRAS G12C inhibitor in KRAS G12C-mutant advanced solid tumors: a first-in-human study.

> **英文摘要：**
> This multicenter, first-in-human Phase 1 study (NCT04956640) evaluated olomorasib (LY3537982), a next-generation KRAS G12C inhibitor designed to enhance target occupancy at low absolute exposures. In total, data from 195 patients are reported: Phase 1a dose escalation (n = 112) assessed olomorasib monotherapy at 50, 100, 150 or 200 mg BID across KRAS G12C-mutant advanced solid tumors; the primary objective was to determine the recommended Phase 2 dose (RP2D) based on dose-limiting toxicities (DLTs). No DLTs occurred, and 150 mg BID was selected as the RP2D. The primary objective for the Phase 1b dose expansion (n = 83) was to evaluate the safety and tolerability of olomorasib in specific KRAS G12C-mutant tumor types. Olomorasib was well tolerated, with predominantly grade 1-2 treatment-related adverse events (TRAEs) and infrequent grade 3 TRAEs; no grade 4/5 TRAEs occurred. Secondary objectives evaluated the antitumor activity of olomorasib. Among 168 efficacy-evaluable patients, the ORR and median PFS were both higher in non-CRC solid tumors compared to CRC, including in patients with NSCLC who previously received a KRAS G12C inhibitor. Intracranial responses were observed in patients with untreated, active brain metastases. This may support the potential of next-generation KRAS G12C inhibitors to overcome limitations of earlier agents and justify further investigation of combination therapy.

> **中文摘要：**
> 这项多中心、首次人体1期研究（NCT04956640）评估了olomorasib（LY3537982），这是一种旨在低绝对暴露下增强靶点占位的新一代KRAS G12C抑制剂。总共报告了195例患者的数据：1a期剂量递增（n = 112）评估了olomorasib单药治疗（50、100、150或200 mg，每日两次）在KRAS G12C突变晚期实体瘤中的情况；主要目的是根据剂量限制性毒性（DLTs）确定推荐的2期剂量（RP2D）。未发生DLTs，150 mg每日两次被选为RP2D。1b期剂量扩展（n = 83）的主要目的是评估olomorasib在特定KRAS G12C突变肿瘤类型中的安全性和耐受性。Olomorasib耐受性良好，主要为1-2级治疗相关不良事件（TRAEs），3级TRAEs少见；未发生4/5级TRAEs。次要目的评估了olomorasib的抗肿瘤活性。在168例可评估疗效的患者中，非结直肠癌（CRC）实体瘤的客观缓解率（ORR）和中位无进展生存期（PFS）均高于CRC患者，包括既往接受过KRAS G12C抑制剂治疗的非小细胞肺癌（NSCLC）患者。在未经治疗的活跃脑转移患者中观察到了颅内缓解。这可能支持新一代KRAS G12C抑制剂具有克服早期药物局限性的潜力，并为进一步研究联合疗法提供了依据。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究是一项首次人体1期临床试验，核心目的是评估新一代KRAS G12C抑制剂olomorasib在晚期实体瘤中的安全性、耐受性及初步抗肿瘤活性。研究采用剂量递增与扩展设计，成功确定了推荐2期剂量，并证实该药物在广泛瘤种中耐受性良好。关键发现包括其在非CRC肿瘤（包括经治NSCLC）中显示出优于CRC的疗效，并观察到颅内活性，这提示其可能克服第一代药物的某些耐药性和中枢神经系统穿透性限制。然而，作为早期研究，其样本量有限，且缺乏与现有标准疗法的直接比较数据，其长期疗效和最佳联合策略仍需后续研究验证。

## 66. 外显子包含特征可实现剪接因子活性的准确估计。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41820334)
**期刊：** Nature communications
**PMID：** 41820334
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41467-026-69642-3

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Exon inclusion signatures enable accurate estimation of splicing factor activity.

> **英文摘要：**
> Splicing factors control exon inclusion in messenger RNAs, shaping transcriptome and proteome diversity. Their catalytic activity is regulated by multiple layers, making single-omic measurements on their own fall short in identifying which splicing factors underlie a phenotype. Here, we posit that splicing factor activity, defined as a splicing factor's ability to modulate exon inclusion, can be estimated from changes in exon inclusion signatures. To test this hypothesis, we benchmark methods for constructing splicing factor→exon networks and estimating splicing factor activity. We find that combining RNA-seq perturbation-based networks with VIPER (Virtual Inference of Protein Activity by Enriched Regulon analysis) accurately captures splicing factor activity as modulated by multiple regulatory layers. This approach integrates splicing factor regulation into a single score derived solely from exon inclusion signatures, allowing functional interpretation of heterogeneous conditions. As a proof of concept, we identify recurrent cancer splicing programs, revealing associations with oncogenic- and tumor suppressor-like splicing factors missed by conventional methods. These programs correlate with patient survival and key cancer hallmarks: initiation, proliferation, and immune evasion. Altogether, we show splicing factor activity can be accurately estimated from exon inclusion changes, enabling comprehensive analyses of splicing regulation with minimal data requirements.

> **中文摘要：**
> 剪接因子通过控制信使RNA中的外显子包含，塑造了转录组和蛋白质组的多样性。它们的催化活性受到多层次的调控，使得单一组学测量本身难以确定哪些剪接因子是表型的基础。在此，我们提出，剪接因子活性（定义为剪接因子调节外显子包含的能力）可以从外显子包含特征的变化中估算出来。为了验证这一假设，我们对构建剪接因子→外显子网络和估算剪接因子活性的方法进行了基准测试。我们发现，将基于RNA-seq扰动的网络与VIPER（通过富集调控子分析进行蛋白质活性的虚拟推断）相结合，能够准确捕捉受多层调控的剪接因子活性。该方法将剪接因子调控整合为一个仅从外显子包含特征衍生的单一评分，从而允许对异质性条件进行功能解读。作为概念验证，我们识别了复发性癌症剪接程序，揭示了传统方法所遗漏的与致癌样和抑癌样剪接因子的关联。这些程序与患者生存以及关键的癌症标志：起始、增殖和免疫逃逸相关。总之，我们表明可以从外显子包含变化中准确估算剪接因子活性，从而能够以最小的数据需求对剪接调控进行全面分析。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在解决剪接因子活性因多层调控而难以通过单一组学数据直接评估的问题。其核心创新在于提出并验证了一种基于外显子包含特征变化来估算剪接因子活性的计算框架，该方法整合了基于扰动的RNA-seq网络与VIPER算法，将复杂的多层调控信息浓缩为单一活性评分。该策略不仅提升了从表型中推断关键剪接因子的能力，还在癌症研究中成功识别了与生存和核心癌症特征相关的、传统方法易忽略的剪接程序，为理解剪接调控提供了高效的分析工具。其局限性可能在于该方法对构建高质量剪接因子-外显子调控网络的依赖，以及在非模型系统或罕见剪接事件中的普适性有待进一步验证。

---

## 67. 基于IPSS-R、IPSS-M和国际共识分类，探讨骨髓增生异常综合征遗传与转录组异常的预后意义

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41820333)
**期刊：** Blood cancer journal
**PMID：** 41820333
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41408-026-01456-4

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Prognostic implications of genetic and transcriptomic abnormalities in MDS according to IPSS-R, IPSS-M, and the International Consensus Classification.

> **英文摘要：**
> Cytogenetic abnormalities and recurrent gene mutations are central to the biology and prognosis of myelodysplastic syndromes/neoplasms (MDS); however, the significance of patients without detectable genomic lesions remains unclear. In this retrospective analysis of 758 patients with primary MDS, the participants were stratified according to the presence of gene mutations and/or cytogenetic abnormalities. Approximately twenty percent lacked both abnormalities and were characterized by younger age, female predominance, lower IPSS-R/IPSS-M risk, and the most favorable survival outcomes. Bulk RNA sequencing further revealed that mutation-negative/normal-karyotype MDS was characterized by immune-metabolic transcriptional programs, whereas genomically altered disease exhibited inflammatory, proliferative, and stress-response signatures, indicating a biologically distinct low-risk state. Therefore, patients without genomic abnormalities appear to constitute a biologically distinct subgroup of MDS. To refine risk assessment beyond IPSS-M systems, a multivariable Cox-based nomogram was developed incorporating age, ferritin level >800 ng/mL, lactate dehydrogenase level >200 U/L, bone marrow fibrosis, and IPSS-M. The proposed model outperformed IPSS-M alone and remained robust following bootstrap validation, allowing individualized 12- and 36-month survival estimation. These findings underscore the limitations of relying solely on molecular assays for risk stratification and support the integration of clinical, genomic, and model-based predictors to improve classification and guide individualized MDS management.

> **中文摘要：**
> 细胞遗传学异常和复发性基因突变是骨髓增生异常综合征/肿瘤（MDS）生物学和预后的核心；然而，未检测到基因组病变的患者的意义仍不清楚。在这项对758例原发性MDS患者的回顾性分析中，参与者根据是否存在基因突变和/或细胞遗传学异常进行分层。大约百分之二十的患者缺乏这两种异常，其特征是年龄较轻、女性占优势、IPSS-R/IPSS-M风险较低，以及最有利的生存结局。批量RNA测序进一步揭示，突变阴性/正常核型MDS的特征是免疫-代谢转录程序，而基因组改变的疾病则表现出炎症、增殖和应激反应特征，表明这是一种生物学上独特的低风险状态。因此，无基因组异常的患者似乎构成了一个生物学上独特的MDS亚组。为了在IPSS-M系统之外完善风险评估，我们开发了一个基于多变量Cox的列线图，纳入了年龄、铁蛋白水平>800 ng/mL、乳酸脱氢酶水平>200 U/L、骨髓纤维化和IPSS-M。所提出的模型优于单独的IPSS-M，并且在Bootstrap验证后保持稳健，允许进行个体化的12个月和36个月生存估计。这些发现强调了仅依赖分子检测进行风险分层的局限性，并支持整合临床、基因组和基于模型的预测因子，以改进分类并指导个体化的MDS管理。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在探讨无基因组异常MDS患者的生物学特征与预后，并构建超越现有IPSS-M系统的个体化风险预测模型。研究通过回顾性分析758例患者，结合基因组分层和转录组测序，识别出一个具有独特免疫代谢特征、预后良好的低风险亚组。其创新性在于整合了临床、基因组及转录组数据，构建了包含年龄、铁蛋白等临床指标的列线图，实现了更精准的个体化生存预测。然而，作为一项回顾性研究，其结论有待前瞻性队列验证，且模型纳入的临床指标（如铁蛋白）可能受多种因素影响，需在更广泛人群中评估其普适性。

---

## 68. 用于卒中区室特异性药物递送的双刚度纳米颗粒。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41820331)
**期刊：** Nature communications
**PMID：** 41820331
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41467-026-70340-3

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Dual-stiffness nanoparticles for compartment-specific drug delivery in stroke.

> **英文摘要：**
> Ischemic stroke presents a dual therapeutic challenge, involving dynamic and compartmentalized pathology in both the peripheral immune system and the central nervous system. Departing from conventional holistic treatment strategies, we developed a spatially tiered drug delivery approach using a combination of dual-stiffness nanoparticles (NPs) for compartment-specific therapy. Exploiting stiffness-dependent biodistribution, stiff NPs preferentially targeted peripheral immune cells, delivering anti-inflammatory agents to attenuate systemic inflammation and prevent immune cell infiltration into the brain. In parallel, soft NPs, shielded from immune uptake, efficiently penetrated the brain to deliver neuroprotectants and restore the damaged neural microenvironment. Mechanistic studies indicate that this selective distribution arises from the interplay between NP stiffness-dependent membrane energetics and competitive serum protein adsorption. This mechano-guided delivery strategy achieves synergistic "peripheral-central" intervention via a single administration, establishing a paradigm for precision nanomedicine, with broad potential in treating multi-compartment pathologies.

> **中文摘要：**
> 缺血性卒中提出了双重治疗挑战，涉及外周免疫系统和中枢神经系统中动态且区室化的病理过程。我们摒弃了传统的整体治疗策略，开发了一种利用双刚度纳米颗粒组合的空间分层药物递送方法，以实现区室特异性治疗。利用刚度依赖的生物分布特性，刚性纳米颗粒优先靶向外周免疫细胞，递送抗炎药物以减轻全身炎症并阻止免疫细胞向大脑浸润。与此同时，柔软的纳米颗粒能够避免被免疫系统摄取，从而有效穿透大脑，递送神经保护剂并修复受损的神经微环境。机制研究表明，这种选择性分布源于纳米颗粒刚度依赖的膜能量学与竞争性血清蛋白吸附之间的相互作用。这种力学引导的递送策略通过单次给药实现了协同的“外周-中枢”干预，为精准纳米医学建立了范式，在治疗多区室病理方面具有广泛潜力。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在解决缺血性卒中治疗中同时针对外周免疫和中枢神经系统的双重挑战。其核心创新在于开发了一种基于纳米颗粒力学性质（刚度）的空间分层递送策略，利用刚性颗粒靶向外周免疫细胞以抗炎，柔软颗粒穿透血脑屏障以神经保护。研究发现，这种选择性分布源于颗粒刚度与膜能量学及血清蛋白吸附的相互作用。该策略通过单次给药实现了外周与中枢的协同干预，为精准纳米医学提供了新范式，但其体内长期安全性与临床转化潜力仍需进一步评估。

---

## 69. CDX2通过上调NUPR1赋予II-III期结肠癌铁死亡抗性。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41820294)
**期刊：** Cell death & disease
**PMID：** 41820294
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41419-026-08412-x

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** CDX2 confers ferroptosis resistance in stage II-III colon cancer via upregulation of NUPR1.

> **英文摘要：**
> High CDX2 expression frequently indicates better survival in stage II-III colon cancer; nevertheless, it is linked to decreased systemic chemotherapy response rates. Ferroptosis, commonly recognized as an iron-dependent oxidative death, is increasingly believed as a disease-modifying mechanism. The purpose of this study is to determine the role of ferroptosis in CDX2-mediated colon cancer chemical resistance. Mechanistically, CDX2-mediated NUPR1 transcription prevents ferroptotic cell death by reducing iron accumulation and oxidative stress damage. Depletion of NUPR1 counteracted the effect of CDX2 overexpression in terms of ferroptosis resistance, whereas transfection-enforced re-expression of NUPR1 restores ferroptosis resistance in CDX2-deficient cells. Genetic or pharmacological blockage of CDX2-NUPR1 axis improved the potential of ferroptosis agonists to combat colon cancer in preclinical mouse models. Our study uncovered a novel molecular mechanism by which CDX2 imparts ferroptosis resistance to colon cancer. Blockage of NUPR1 might be as a potential therapeutic strategy for CDX2-positive stage II-III colon cancer.The current study demonstrated a positive correlation between CDX2 expression and chemical resistance in colon cancer. Mechanistically, CDX2 directly transactivates NUPR1 and subsequent its target LCN2 to confer ferroptosis resistance by inhibiting iron-induced oxidative damage. Genetic or pharmacological blockage of CDX2-NUPR1 axis may strengthen the anticancer efficacy of adjuvant chemotherapy on stage II-III CDX2-positive colon cancer in vitro and in vivo. Our study uncovered a novel molecular mechanism by which CDX2 confers ferroptosis resistance in colon cancer. Blockage of NUPR1 might be as a potential therapeutic strategy for stage II-III CDX2-positive colon cancer.

> **中文摘要：**
> 高CDX2表达通常预示着II-III期结肠癌患者更好的生存率；然而，它也与全身化疗反应率降低相关。铁死亡，通常被认为是一种铁依赖的氧化性死亡，正日益被视为一种疾病修饰机制。本研究旨在确定铁死亡在CDX2介导的结肠癌化疗耐药中的作用。从机制上讲，CDX2介导的NUPR1转录通过减少铁积累和氧化应激损伤来阻止铁死亡性细胞死亡。NUPR1的耗竭抵消了CDX2过表达在铁死亡抗性方面的作用，而通过转染强制重新表达NUPR1则可在CDX2缺陷细胞中恢复铁死亡抗性。在临床前小鼠模型中，基因或药理学阻断CDX2-NUPR1轴提高了铁死亡激动剂对抗结肠癌的潜力。我们的研究揭示了CDX2赋予结肠癌铁死亡抗性的新分子机制。阻断NUPR1可能作为CDX2阳性II-III期结肠癌的潜在治疗策略。本研究证实了结肠癌中CDX2表达与化疗耐药性之间存在正相关。从机制上讲，CDX2直接反式激活NUPR1及其后续靶标LCN2，通过抑制铁诱导的氧化损伤来赋予铁死亡抗性。基因或药理学阻断CDX2-NUPR1轴可能在体外和体内增强辅助化疗对II-III期CDX2阳性结肠癌的抗癌疗效。我们的研究揭示了CDX2赋予结肠癌铁死亡抗性的新分子机制。阻断NUPR1可能作为II-III期CDX2阳性结肠癌的潜在治疗策略。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在阐明CDX2高表达与II-III期结肠癌化疗耐药关联的分子机制，核心发现CDX2通过转录激活NUPR1-LCN2轴抑制铁死亡，从而赋予肿瘤细胞耐药性。研究采用基因敲除/过回补、药理学干预及临床前动物模型，方法体系较为完整。其创新性在于首次将CDX2的预后保护作用与其诱导的化疗耐药性通过铁死亡机制联系起来，并提出了靶向NUPR1以逆转耐药的治疗新策略。局限性在于摘要未提及临床样本验证细节，且NUPR1抑制剂的选择性与毒性有待进一步评估。

---

## 70. ONC206展现出强大的抗肿瘤活性，是治疗高危髓母细胞瘤的一种潜在新型治疗策略。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41818696)
**期刊：** Neuro-oncology
**PMID：** 41818696
**DOI：** 10.1093/neuonc/noag053

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** ONC206 demonstrates potent anti-tumorigenic activity and is a potential novel therapeutic strategy for high-risk medulloblastoma.

> **英文摘要：**
> BACKGROUND: Medulloblastoma is the most common malignant pediatric brain tumor, and has an urgent need for novel treatment approaches. Dordaviprone (ONC201) and its chemical derivative with nanomolar potency, ONC206, induce apoptosis of cancer cells by activation of the mitochondrial caseinolytic protease P (ClpP). ONC206 is currently in Phase I clinical trials for pediatric patients with primary brain tumors.
> 
> METHODS: In this study, we evaluated the preclinical therapeutic effects of ONC206 in medulloblastoma and investigated its mechanism of action.
> 
> RESULTS: We found evidence for high expression of ClpP at both the RNA and protein level in medulloblastoma tumors, compared to very low expression in normal brain tissue. In addition, we saw a pronounced reduction in cell viability of human Group 3 and Group 4 and murine SHH-driven and Group 3 medulloblastoma cells treated with ONC206 with low IC-50s. After treatment with ONC206, we observed an induction of integrated stress response and mitochondrial damage. To test the efficacy of ONC206 in vivo, we used murine models of SHH-driven and Group 3 medulloblastoma as well as Group 3 and Group 4 patient-derived xenografts (PDXs). ONC206 led to a significant prolongation of survival in both murine models, with the SHH mice demonstrating survival extension from 70 to 140 days. PDX-bearing mice also responded to ONC206, which led to a significant survival benefit.
> 
> CONCLUSION: Our results highlight ONC206 as a novel therapeutic option for patients with high-risk medulloblastoma and provide strong rationale for testing the efficacy of ONC206 in the treatment of these patients.

> **中文摘要：**
> 背景：髓母细胞瘤是最常见的儿童恶性脑肿瘤，迫切需要新的治疗方法。Dordaviprone (ONC201) 及其具有纳摩尔效力的化学衍生物 ONC206，通过激活线粒体酪蛋白水解蛋白酶 P (ClpP) 来诱导癌细胞凋亡。ONC206目前正在针对患有原发性脑肿瘤的儿科患者进行I期临床试验。
> 
> 方法：在本研究中，我们评估了ONC206在髓母细胞瘤中的临床前治疗效果，并研究了其作用机制。
> 
> 结果：我们发现，与正常脑组织中极低的表达水平相比，髓母细胞瘤肿瘤中ClpP在RNA和蛋白水平均呈高表达。此外，我们观察到经ONC206处理后，人类第3组和第4组以及小鼠SHH驱动型和第3组髓母细胞瘤细胞的活力显著降低，且IC-50值较低。在用ONC206处理后，我们观察到整合应激反应和线粒体损伤的诱导。为了在体内测试ONC206的疗效，我们使用了SHH驱动型和第3组髓母细胞瘤的小鼠模型，以及第3组和第4组患者来源的异种移植瘤(PDX)模型。ONC206显著延长了两种小鼠模型的生存期，其中SHH小鼠的生存期从70天延长至140天。携带PDX的小鼠也对ONC206产生反应，获得了显著的生存获益。
> 
> 结论：我们的研究结果强调了ONC206作为高危髓母细胞瘤患者的一种新型治疗选择，并为测试ONC206治疗这些患者的疗效提供了强有力的依据。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在评估新型化合物ONC206治疗高危髓母细胞瘤的临床前潜力。研究通过验证靶点ClpP在肿瘤中的高表达，结合体外细胞毒性实验（低IC-50值）和体内多种动物模型（包括基因工程鼠和PDX模型），系统性地证明了ONC206通过激活ClpP、诱导整合应激反应和线粒体损伤，从而有效抑制肿瘤生长并显著延长生存期。其创新性在于为ONC201的衍生物ONC206提供了针对髓母细胞瘤（特别是高危亚型）的强效证据，并揭示了其作用机制，为正在进行的I期临床试验提供了重要支持。局限性在于，摘要未提及ONC206对正常组织的潜在毒性、药代动力学细节以及与其他疗法的联合应用效果，这些是未来临床转化中需要关注的关键问题。

---

## 71. 评估“脑渗透性”：原发性与转移性脑肿瘤治疗药物研发的关键问题

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41818680)
**期刊：** Neuro-oncology
**PMID：** 41818680
**DOI：** 10.1093/neuonc/noag051

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Evaluating "Brain Permeability": A Critical Issue for the Development of Therapeutic Agents for Primary and Metastatic Brain Tumors.

> **英文摘要：**
> Current assessments of brain permeability rely predominantly on drug delivery to contrast-enhancing tumor regions. However, substantial portions of central nervous system (CNS) tumors reside within non-enhancing brain (NEB), where drug concentrations frequently remain subtherapeutic. This collaborative Adult Brain Tumor Consortium and Food and Drug Administration workshop aimed to identify criteria for defining NEB permeability to accomplish two critical objectives: 1) allocate clinical trial resources toward agents achieving therapeutic NEB concentrations and 2) minimize systemic toxicity when CNS benefit is improbable. The workshop systematically evaluated permeability assessment modalities, including drug physicochemical properties, in vitro blood-brain barrier models, and penetration into cerebrospinal fluid and normal rodent brain. Methodological approaches to determine requisite NEB drug concentrations and approaches to measuring NEB pharmacokinetics and pharmacodynamics were examined. This culminated in developing the Non-Enhancing Brain Permeability Index (NEBPI), which assigns therapeutic agents to three categories: sufficiently permeable, insufficiently permeable, or impermeable. The NEBPI provides a standardized framework to assist investigators and regulatory agencies to evaluate NEB penetration before human efficacy studies are initiated for agents that require direct tumor contact. Assessing NEB drug penetration is critical to improving outcomes in CNS tumors and reducing the incidence of brain metastases in systemic malignancies.

> **中文摘要：**
> 目前对脑渗透性的评估主要依赖于药物向对比增强肿瘤区域的递送。然而，中枢神经系统（CNS）肿瘤的相当大部分位于非增强脑（NEB）区域，该区域的药物浓度常常达不到治疗水平。本次成人脑肿瘤联盟与美国食品药品监督管理局联合举办的研讨会，旨在确定定义NEB渗透性的标准，以实现两个关键目标：1）将临床试验资源分配给能达到治疗性NEB浓度的药物；2）在CNS获益可能性不大时，最大限度地减少全身毒性。研讨会系统评估了渗透性评估方法，包括药物的理化性质、体外血脑屏障模型、以及向脑脊液和正常啮齿动物脑的渗透。会议还审查了确定所需NEB药物浓度的方法，以及测量NEB药代动力学和药效学的方法。最终，会议制定了非增强脑渗透性指数（NEBPI），该指数将治疗药物分为三类：渗透充分、渗透不足或不渗透。NEBPI提供了一个标准化框架，可帮助研究者和监管机构在启动需要直接接触肿瘤的药物的人体疗效研究之前，评估其NEB渗透性。评估药物的NEB渗透对于改善CNS肿瘤的治疗效果和降低全身性恶性肿瘤的脑转移发生率至关重要。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

该研讨会旨在解决脑肿瘤药物研发中一个关键但常被忽视的难题：如何评估药物对非增强脑（NEB）区域的渗透性。其核心创新在于系统整合了多种评估方法，并最终提出了一个标准化的分类框架——非增强脑渗透性指数（NEBPI）。该指数为药物研发和监管决策提供了前瞻性工具，有助于优化临床试验资源配置并降低无效治疗带来的全身毒性。然而，其局限性在于NEBPI的验证和临床应用仍需大量前瞻性研究数据支持，且评估方法（如体外模型和动物模型）与人体真实情况的关联性仍需进一步确认。

---

## 75. 帕博利珠单抗联合或不联合仑伐替尼作为复发或转移性头颈部鳞状细胞癌一线治疗：III期LEAP-010研究。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41818638)
**期刊：** Journal of clinical oncology : official journal of the American Society of Clinical Oncology
**PMID：** 41818638
**DOI：** 10.1200/JCO-25-00570

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Pembrolizumab With or Without Lenvatinib as First-Line Therapy for Recurrent or Metastatic Head and Neck Squamous Cell Carcinoma: Phase III LEAP-010 Study.

> **英文摘要：**
> PURPOSE: The PD-1 inhibitor pembrolizumab is approved as first-line treatment for recurrent/metastatic head and neck squamous cell carcinoma (R/M HNSCC). In LEAP-010 (ClinicalTrials.gov identifier: NCT04199104), the multikinase inhibitor lenvatinib plus pembrolizumab was evaluated as first-line therapy in participants with PD-L1 combined positive score (CPS) ≥1 R/M HNSCC.
> 
> METHODS: In this phase III, randomized, placebo-controlled, double-blind study, participants 18 years and older with PD-L1 CPS ≥1 R/M HNSCC deemed incurable by local therapy were randomly assigned 1:1 to lenvatinib 20 mg plus pembrolizumab 200 mg IV once every 3 weeks for ≤35 cycles or placebo orally once daily plus pembrolizumab 200 mg IV once every 3 weeks for ≤35 cycles. Primary end points were objective response rate (ORR), progression-free survival (PFS), and overall survival (OS). Per the prespecified analysis plan, ORR and PFS were reported from the first interim analysis (IA1; data cutoff: July 6, 2022), and OS from IA2 (data cutoff: May 30, 2023).
> 
> RESULTS: Five hundred eleven participants were randomly assigned to lenvatinib plus pembrolizumab (n = 256) or placebo plus pembrolizumab (n = 255). The median time from random assignment to data cutoff was 11.5 months for IA1 and 21.3 months for IA2. At IA1, the median PFS was 6.2 months for lenvatinib plus pembrolizumab versus 2.8 months for placebo plus pembrolizumab (hazard ratio [HR], 0.64 [95% CI, 0.50 to 0.81];  = .0001040); the ORR was 46.1% versus 25.4%, respectively (difference = 20.2% [95% CI, 10.5 to 29.6];  = .0000251). At IA2, the median OS was 15.0 months for lenvatinib plus pembrolizumab versus 17.9 months for placebo plus pembrolizumab (HR,1.15 [95% CI, 0.91 to 1.45];  = .882). At IA2, 170 (66.9%) participants receiving lenvatinib plus pembrolizumab had grade 3-4 all-cause adverse events compared with 97 (38.3%) participants on placebo plus pembrolizumab.
> 
> CONCLUSION: In participants with PD-L1 CPS ≥1 R/M HNSCC, first-line lenvatinib plus pembrolizumab significantly improved ORR and PFS, but not OS, compared with placebo plus pembrolizumab. The safety profile was consistent with published data.

> **中文摘要：**
> 目的：PD-1抑制剂帕博利珠单抗已被批准用于复发/转移性头颈部鳞状细胞癌（R/M HNSCC）的一线治疗。在LEAP-010研究（ClinicalTrials.gov标识符：NCT04199104）中，评估了多激酶抑制剂仑伐替尼联合帕博利珠单抗作为PD-L1联合阳性评分（CPS）≥1的R/M HNSCC参与者的一线治疗。
> 
> 方法：在这项III期、随机、安慰剂对照、双盲研究中，年龄≥18岁、PD-L1 CPS ≥1、经局部治疗被认为无法治愈的R/M HNSCC参与者，按1:1随机分配接受仑伐替尼20 mg口服每日一次联合帕博利珠单抗200 mg静脉注射每3周一次（≤35个周期），或安慰剂口服每日一次联合帕博利珠单抗200 mg静脉注射每3周一次（≤35个周期）。主要终点是客观缓解率（ORR）、无进展生存期（PFS）和总生存期（OS）。根据预设分析计划，ORR和PFS数据来自第一次中期分析（IA1；数据截止日期：2022年7月6日），OS数据来自第二次中期分析（IA2；数据截止日期：2023年5月30日）。
> 
> 结果：511名参与者被随机分配至仑伐替尼联合帕博利珠单抗组（n = 256）或安慰剂联合帕博利珠单抗组（n = 255）。从随机分配到数据截止的中位时间，IA1为11.5个月，IA2为21.3个月。在IA1时，仑伐替尼联合帕博利珠单抗组的中位PFS为6.2个月，而安慰剂联合帕博利珠单抗组为2.8个月（风险比[HR]，0.64 [95% CI，0.50至0.81]；P = .0001040）；ORR分别为46.1%和25.4%（差异=20.2% [95% CI，10.5至29.6]；P = .0000251）。在IA2时，仑伐替尼联合帕博利珠单抗组的中位OS为15.0个月，而安慰剂联合帕博利珠单抗组为17.9个月（HR，1.15 [95% CI，0.91至1.45]；P = .882）。在IA2时，接受仑伐替尼联合帕博利珠单抗的参与者中有170名（66.9%）发生了3-4级全因不良事件，而安慰剂联合帕博利珠单抗组为97名（38.3%）。
> 
> 结论：在PD-L1 CPS ≥1的R/M HNSCC参与者中，与安慰剂联合帕博利珠单抗相比，一线仑伐替尼联合帕博利珠单抗显著改善了ORR和PFS，但未改善OS。安全性特征与已发表数据一致。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在评估仑伐替尼联合帕博利珠单抗对比帕博利珠单抗单药在PD-L1阳性R/M HNSCC一线治疗中的疗效与安全性。这是一项设计严谨的III期随机双盲安慰剂对照试验，主要终点包括ORR、PFS和OS。结果显示，联合治疗组在ORR和PFS方面取得了具有统计学意义的显著改善，但未能转化为总生存获益，且联合组3-4级不良事件发生率显著更高。该研究创新性地探索了免疫联合抗血管生成靶向治疗在此类患者中的应用，但其核心局限性在于OS未获益且毒性增加，这提示联合方案未能克服免疫单药治疗的生存瓶颈，并为临床决策提供了重要的风险效益权衡依据。

---

## 76. 基于CRISPR/Cas9的钒基MXene自由基时空可控纳米反应器用于光热诱导的多效应协同抗肿瘤治疗

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41818620)
**期刊：** Advanced science (Weinheim, Baden-Wurttemberg, Germany)
**PMID：** 41818620
**DOI：** 10.1002/advs.202522535

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** CRISPR/Cas9-Based Vanadium MXene-Free Radical Spatiotemporally Controlled Nanoreactor for Photothermal-Induced Multi-Effect Synergistic Antitumor Therapy.

> **英文摘要：**
> Photothermal therapy (PTT), a non-invasive tumor treatment, shows promise but is limited in solid tumors by restricted tissue penetration, thermotolerance, anti-apoptotic and immunosuppressive effects. In this study, tumor microenvironment-responsive nanoplatform VARH was constructed based on MXene. Under NIR-II laser irradiation, VARH achieves a high photothermal conversion efficiency of 44.21%. Loaded 2,2'-azobis[2-(2-imidazolin-2-yl)propane] dihydrochloride decomposes at high temperatures to generate alkyl radicals, synergizing with hydroxyl radicals from V-catalyzed endogenous HO decomposition, enabling chemodynamic therapy (CDT) and thermal dynamic therapy to enhance tumor cell oxidative damage. Triggered by high glutathione, VARH releases ribonucleoprotein (RNP) complexes to knockout heat shock protein 90 (HSP90), attenuating cellular heat resistance and promoting apoptosis. It also enhances T cell-mediated anti-tumor immunity and, with free radicals, promotes tumor cell immunogenic cell death (ICD), achieving immunotherapeutic multi-effect synergy. Integrating nanotechnology with precise gene editing, this study develops a novel multimodal synergistic therapy system, providing new insights for multi-modal treatment R&D and advancing PTT and free radical-based cancer therapies.

> **中文摘要：**
> 光热疗法（PTT）作为一种非侵入性肿瘤治疗方法，前景广阔，但在实体瘤中受到组织穿透受限、热耐受、抗凋亡和免疫抑制效应的限制。本研究基于MXene构建了肿瘤微环境响应型纳米平台VARH。在NIR-II激光照射下，VARH实现了44.21%的高光热转换效率。负载的2,2'-偶氮二[2-(2-咪唑啉-2-基)丙烷]二盐酸盐在高温下分解产生烷基自由基，与V催化内源性H2O2分解产生的羟基自由基协同作用，实现化学动力学疗法（CDT）和热动力学疗法，增强肿瘤细胞氧化损伤。在高浓度谷胱甘肽触发下，VARH释放核糖核蛋白（RNP）复合物以敲除热休克蛋白90（HSP90），减弱细胞耐热性并促进细胞凋亡。它还能增强T细胞介导的抗肿瘤免疫，并与自由基共同促进肿瘤细胞发生免疫原性细胞死亡（ICD），实现免疫治疗的多效应协同。本研究将纳米技术与精确基因编辑相结合，开发了一种新型多模态协同治疗系统，为多模态治疗研发提供了新见解，并推动了PTT和基于自由基的癌症疗法的发展。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在克服光热疗法在实体瘤治疗中的多重局限，核心是构建一种集光热、自由基动力学与基因编辑于一体的智能纳米平台VARH。其方法创新在于利用MXene的高效光热转换，结合V催化与热敏自由基前体实现时空可控的氧化损伤，并通过CRISPR/Cas9敲除HSP90以破解热耐受。研究发现该系统能协同诱导肿瘤细胞氧化损伤、凋亡及免疫原性死亡，并增强抗肿瘤免疫，实现了多模态协同治疗。主要创新性在于将纳米催化自由基疗法与精准基因编辑有机结合，为肿瘤治疗提供了新范式；局限性可能在于复杂的纳米平台其体内生物安全性、长期毒性和大规模制备工艺仍需深入评估。

---

## 77. 从游离转录组到单细胞图谱：基于图矩阵分解的生物标志物发现与来源细胞改变分析

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41818613)
**期刊：** Advanced science (Weinheim, Baden-Wurttemberg, Germany)
**PMID：** 41818613
**DOI：** 10.1002/advs.74814

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** From Cell-Free Transcriptomes to Single-Cell Landscapes: Biomarker Discovery and Originating Cell Alteration Analysis via Graph Matrix Factorization.

> **英文摘要：**
> Characterizing the cellular origin and disease-driven dynamics of cfRNA is essential for integrating cfRNA profiling into clinical workflows and precision-medicine strategies. Most cfRNA studies are restricted to bulk-level analyses, which preclude detailed analysis of alterations in the cellular origins of cfRNA. Single-cell RNA sequencing reveals cellular heterogeneity and communication, but its application to cfRNA is limited by diverse cellular origins, leaving a critical gap in understanding functional alterations in cfRNA biomarker-originating cells. In this work, we propose CellFreeGMF, a tool designed to enable diagnosis classification of clinical samples, identify cfRNA biomarkers, and analyze the alterations in their originating cells based on graph matrix factorization. Furthermore, by utilizing cell-cell communication analysis, CellFreeGMF investigates the functional alterations occurring in the cfRNA originating cells under disease conditions. We validate CellFreeGMF on diverse cell-free RNA transcriptome clinical datasets. In the case of pancreatic ductal adenocarcinoma (PDAC), CellFreeGMF not only identified cfRNA biomarkers but also traced their cellular origins to myeloid and T-cell populations. Further analysis revealed significant transcriptomic differences in these cell populations between disease and normal groups. Our user-friendly CellFreeGMF toolkit (https://cellfreegmf.readthedocs.io/) enables identifying cfRNA biomarkers and elucidating pathophysiological changes in their originating cells.

> **中文摘要：**
> 阐明细胞游离RNA（cfRNA）的细胞来源及其疾病驱动的动态变化，对于将cfRNA谱分析整合到临床工作流程和精准医疗策略中至关重要。大多数cfRNA研究局限于整体水平分析，这阻碍了对cfRNA细胞来源改变的详细分析。单细胞RNA测序揭示了细胞异质性和细胞间通讯，但其在cfRNA中的应用因cfRNA来源细胞多样而受限，导致在理解cfRNA生物标志物来源细胞的功能改变方面存在关键空白。在本研究中，我们提出了CellFreeGMF，这是一个基于图矩阵分解设计的工具，旨在实现临床样本的诊断分类、识别cfRNA生物标志物并分析其来源细胞的改变。此外，通过利用细胞间通讯分析，CellFreeGMF研究了疾病条件下cfRNA来源细胞中发生的功能改变。我们在多种细胞游离RNA转录组临床数据集上验证了CellFreeGMF。在胰腺导管腺癌（PDAC）案例中，CellFreeGMF不仅识别了cfRNA生物标志物，还将其细胞来源追溯至髓系细胞和T细胞群体。进一步分析揭示了这些细胞群体在疾病组与正常组之间存在显著的转录组差异。我们用户友好的CellFreeGMF工具包（https://cellfreegmf.readthedocs.io/）能够识别cfRNA生物标志物并阐明其来源细胞的病理生理变化。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在解决游离RNA（cfRNA）研究中细胞来源解析不足的关键问题。其核心是开发了名为CellFreeGMF的计算工具，该工具创新性地结合图矩阵分解与细胞通讯分析，不仅实现了基于cfRNA的疾病诊断分类和生物标志物识别，更关键的是能追溯标志物的细胞来源并分析这些来源细胞在疾病状态下的功能改变。在胰腺癌数据中的验证表明，该方法能将cfRNA标志物溯源至髓系细胞和T细胞，并揭示其转录组差异，为理解疾病机制提供了新视角。其局限性在于方法依赖于外部单细胞图谱的准确性和完整性，且分析结果需进一步的实验验证。

---

## 78. 冷冻消融通过激活巨噬细胞中的cGAS-STING-CXCL10轴增强非小细胞肺癌的抗肿瘤免疫。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41818612)
**期刊：** Advanced science (Weinheim, Baden-Wurttemberg, Germany)
**PMID：** 41818612
**DOI：** 10.1002/advs.202521931

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Cryoablation Activates the cGAS-STING-CXCL10 Axis in Macrophages to Enhance Anti-Tumor Immunity in NSCLC.

> **英文摘要：**
> Local ablative therapy has emerged as an essential treatment for patients with non-small cell lung cancer (NSCLC). Whether cryoablation is superior to thermal ablation in the era of immunotherapy and the related mechanism remains undefined. We first observed superior progression-free survival with cryoablation compared with thermal ablation in patients with oligoresidual disease after immunotherapy. Single-cell RNA sequencing of human peripheral blood monocyte cells and mouse tumors showed that cryoablation combined with anti-PD-1 expanded more CXCL10 macrophages than thermal ablation combination. CXCR3 blockade and inhibition of T cells egressing from draining lymph nodes abolished the systemic anti-tumor efficacy. Mechanistically, tumor DNA released by cryoablation was taken up by macrophages, activating the cGAS-STING signaling pathway, increasing the pool of CXCL10 macrophages and CXCL10 secretion. Our study demonstrated that CXCL10 macrophages and the CXCR3 T cells were critical mediators of the systemic anti-tumor immunity induced by cryoablation in advanced NSCLC.

> **中文摘要：**
> 局部消融治疗已成为非小细胞肺癌患者的重要治疗手段。在免疫治疗时代，冷冻消融是否优于热消融及其相关机制尚不明确。我们首先观察到，在免疫治疗后寡残留病灶患者中，冷冻消融相较于热消融显示出更优的无进展生存期。对人外周血单核细胞和小鼠肿瘤的单细胞RNA测序显示，冷冻消融联合抗PD-1治疗比热消融联合治疗能扩增更多的CXCL10阳性巨噬细胞。阻断CXCR3或抑制T细胞从引流淋巴结迁出，均会消除这种系统性抗肿瘤疗效。机制上，冷冻消融释放的肿瘤DNA被巨噬细胞摄取，激活了cGAS-STING信号通路，从而增加了CXCL10阳性巨噬细胞池和CXCL10的分泌。我们的研究表明，CXCL10阳性巨噬细胞和CXCR3阳性T细胞是冷冻消融在晚期NSCLC中诱导系统性抗肿瘤免疫的关键介质。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在探索冷冻消融在免疫治疗背景下优于热消融的机制。研究者通过临床观察、单细胞测序和体内外功能实验，系统性地揭示了冷冻消融通过释放肿瘤DNA激活巨噬细胞cGAS-STING通路，进而驱动CXCL10-CXCR3轴，招募T细胞并增强系统性抗肿瘤免疫的新机制。该研究的创新性在于明确了冷冻消融独特的免疫激活通路，为联合治疗策略提供了精准靶点；局限性在于主要发现基于临床前模型和有限临床样本，其临床转化效果及在更广泛人群中的适用性仍需大规模研究验证。

---

## 79. 用于靶向癌症治疗的仿生细胞膜包覆金属有机框架系统。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41818608)
**期刊：** Advanced science (Weinheim, Baden-Wurttemberg, Germany)
**PMID：** 41818608
**DOI：** 10.1002/advs.202521580

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Biomimetic Cell Membrane-Coated MOFs System for Targeted Cancer Therapy.

> **英文摘要：**
> The integration of metal-organic frameworks (MOFs) with cell membrane coatings has emerged as a revolutionary strategy to enhance the therapeutic efficacy of cancer nanomedicine. In this review, we systematically summarized recent advances in cell membrane-camouflaged MOF as drug delivery systems, focusing on their unique advantages in tumor targeting, immune evasion, and biocompatibility. By emulating the characteristics of natural cells, these biomimetic systems demonstrate enhanced circulation time, increased accumulation within tumors, and decreased uptake by macrophages. A critical analysis was conducted on a variety of membrane sources, including cancer cells, red blood cells, and macrophages. The analysis focused on the functionalities of these sources in tumor homing and immune modulation. The following design strategies are of particular interest: hybrid membrane engineering and stimuli-responsive drug release mechanisms. This field demonstrates considerable potential for combination therapies integrating chemotherapy, immunotherapy, and photothermal modalities. In the future, the development of new drugs should prioritize intelligent drug release systems and personalized treatment through advanced biomaterial engineering.

> **中文摘要：**
> 金属有机框架（MOFs）与细胞膜涂层的整合已成为一种革命性策略，旨在提升癌症纳米药物的治疗效果。本综述系统总结了细胞膜伪装的MOF作为药物递送系统的最新进展，重点关注其在肿瘤靶向、免疫逃逸和生物相容性方面的独特优势。通过模拟天然细胞的特性，这些仿生系统展现出延长的循环时间、增加的肿瘤内积累以及减少的巨噬细胞摄取。我们对多种膜来源（包括癌细胞、红细胞和巨噬细胞）进行了批判性分析。该分析聚焦于这些来源在肿瘤归巢和免疫调节方面的功能。以下设计策略尤其值得关注：杂化膜工程和刺激响应型药物释放机制。该领域在整合化疗、免疫疗法和光热疗法的联合治疗方面展现出巨大潜力。未来，新药的开发应通过先进的生物材料工程，优先发展智能药物释放系统和个性化治疗。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

该综述旨在总结和评价仿生细胞膜包覆金属有机框架（MOFs）这一新兴药物递送系统在癌症治疗中的应用。其核心方法是通过整合MOFs的高载药能力与细胞膜的生物界面特性，构建具有肿瘤靶向、免疫逃逸和生物相容性优势的仿生纳米平台。研究发现，该系统能有效延长循环时间、增加肿瘤富集，并可通过杂化膜工程和刺激响应释放机制实现功能优化，展现出联合多种治疗模式的巨大潜力。其创新性在于巧妙融合了材料科学与生物仿生学，但作为综述，其局限性在于主要总结现有研究，对具体临床转化挑战（如大规模生产、批次稳定性、体内长期安全性）的深入探讨相对有限。

---

## 80. 小胶质细胞Rank信号通路调控GnRH神经元功能及下丘脑-垂体-性腺轴。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41818388)
**期刊：** Science (New York, N.Y.)
**PMID：** 41818388
**DOI：** 10.1126/science.aeb6999

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Microglia Rank signaling regulates GnRH neuronal function and the hypothalamic-pituitary-gonadal axis.

> **英文摘要：**
> The hypothalamic-pituitary-gonadal axis (HPG) controls pubertal development, sexual maturation, and fertility. We identified a role of hypothalamic microglia in controlling the HPG axis through receptor activator of nuclear factor κβ (Rank) signaling. Whole-body and microglia Rank depletion led to hypogonadotropic hypogonadism (HH) resulting from an alteration in gonadotropin-releasing hormone (GnRH) neuron function. In addition, we identified rare gene variants of  in patients with HH. Transcriptional profiling upon Rank loss revealed defective microglia activation and morphological alterations in the median eminence, decreasing the contacts and engulfment of GnRH terminal projections and impairing GnRH neuronal responses to kisspeptin. Overall, our data uncover the microglia as regulator of GnRH neuronal function through Rank signaling, with potential implications for reproductive maturation and fertility.

> **中文摘要：**
> 下丘脑-垂体-性腺轴（HPG）控制着青春期发育、性成熟和生育能力。我们发现下丘脑小胶质细胞通过核因子κB受体活化因子（Rank）信号通路在调控HPG轴中发挥作用。全身性和小胶质细胞特异性Rank缺失导致了低促性腺激素性性腺功能减退症（HH），其源于促性腺激素释放激素（GnRH）神经元功能的改变。此外，我们在HH患者中发现了罕见的基因变异。Rank缺失后的转录谱分析揭示了正中隆起区小胶质细胞激活缺陷和形态学改变，减少了与GnRH末端投射的接触和吞噬，并损害了GnRH神经元对kisspeptin的反应。总之，我们的数据揭示了小胶质细胞通过Rank信号通路作为GnRH神经元功能的调节者，这对生殖成熟和生育能力具有潜在意义。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在揭示小胶质细胞在调控下丘脑-垂体-性腺轴中的新作用。通过结合基因敲除模型、患者基因变异分析和转录组学，研究发现小胶质细胞通过Rank信号通路调节GnRH神经元功能，其机制涉及对GnRH神经元末梢的接触与吞噬。该发现创新性地将神经免疫细胞与生殖神经内分泌调控联系起来，为理解低促性腺激素性性腺功能减退症的病因提供了新视角。然而，研究主要基于动物模型，Rank信号在人类生殖疾病中的具体作用机制及其作为治疗靶点的潜力仍需进一步临床验证。

---

## 81. 在胰腺癌“起飞”前将其击溃

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41818383)
**期刊：** Science (New York, N.Y.)
**PMID：** 41818383
**DOI：** 10.1126/science.aef6665

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** KRAShing pancreatic cancer before takeoff.

> **英文摘要：**
> Drugs that inhibit KRAS signaling delay the development of pancreatic cancer in mice.

> **中文摘要：**
> 抑制KRAS信号传导的药物可延缓小鼠胰腺癌的发生发展。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在探索靶向KRAS信号通路对胰腺癌发生发展的干预效果。研究采用小鼠模型，通过药理学方法抑制KRAS信号。核心发现是，KRAS抑制剂能够显著延缓小鼠胰腺癌的进展。其创新性在于直接验证了在肿瘤形成早期阶段靶向KRAS的预防潜力，为胰腺癌的早期干预提供了概念性证据；主要局限性在于结果源于动物模型，其临床转化效果尚待人体试验验证。

## 82. 拓展经典癌基因的作用范围

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41818382)
**期刊：** Science (New York, N.Y.)
**PMID：** 41818382
**DOI：** 10.1126/science.aef9956

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Extending the reach of a classic oncogene.

> **英文摘要：**
> Exocytosis exposes Src at the outer surface of cancer cells, poised for therapeutic targeting.

> **中文摘要：**
> 胞吐作用使Src暴露于癌细胞的外表面，为治疗靶向做好了准备。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

该研究揭示了经典癌基因Src在肿瘤细胞中的新定位——通过胞吐作用暴露于细胞外表面。这一发现的核心目的是为靶向Src提供新的治疗窗口。其创新性在于将细胞生物学过程（胞吐）与癌蛋白的亚细胞定位及靶向治疗潜力联系起来，提出了一种潜在的新型治疗策略。然而，摘要信息有限，其局限性在于未阐明该暴露过程的具体机制、在不同癌症类型中的普适性以及直接靶向该外露Src分子的具体疗效和安全性，这些均有待后续实验验证。
